Foreign News Two

U.S. Veterans Riot

Throwing Bricks at Police

Troops Deployed to Suppress the Situation

Tear Gas Used to Clear the Chaos, Barracks Set Ablaze

Veterans Empty-Handed Retreat from Washington

Reuters, Washington, 28th – Veterans who have been camping out in the open in the capital for weeks, demanding that the government issue bonus certificates for cash, have suddenly clashed with the police. The veterans threw bricks at the police, who returned fire, causing a serious situation. All the police in the American capital were gathered on Pennsylvania Avenue and other major thoroughfares. In the afternoon, the authorities deployed troops to suppress the situation. A cavalry unit rushed across the Potomac River and headed towards the White House. Upon arrival, they found the police struggling to control the chaos. Two hundred cavalry soldiers and a company of infantry, carrying several machine guns and five armored vehicles, were stationed around the White House, hoping to quickly quell the turmoil. The situation was at its worst this afternoon, but after the soldiers used tear gas, they dispersed the veterans.

Reuters, Washington, 28th – After the troops were deployed near the White House, the infantry advanced quickly with fixed bayonets, dispersing the veterans. Some were unwilling to continue retreating, so the infantry put on gas masks and threw tear gas bombs at the shouting and cursing crowd. Blue smoke filled the air, and the veterans scrambled to escape. The infantry led the way, followed by tanks, clearing the buildings occupied by the veterans. A fire broke out in the temporary shacks where the veterans lived, and the fire brigade was dispatched to extinguish it. An inspection revealed three police officers and one soldier injured, while one veteran was killed and six injured. After the veterans were driven out of Washington, the troops were ordered to clear the veterans' main camp five miles from Washington, where 7,000 veterans lived. The troops first helped 380 women and 488 children out, then used tear gas to disperse the remaining crowd, and then set fire to their tents. More than fifty people were injured on both sides. This operation was commanded by General MacArthur, Chief of Staff of the U.S. Army. National News Agency, Washington, 28th – Today's disturbance began when federal government personnel, accompanied by police, evicted veterans squatting in federal government buildings. Eighteen people advocated resistance, and one climbed onto the roof, waving a flag and calling for support. Veteran leader Walter Waters had agreed to withdraw yesterday and gave a speech urging a peaceful retreat, but the crowd did not listen and rushed past the police cordon, seizing a pile of bricks and engaging in a brick battle with the police for ten minutes. Police Inspector General Glassford, known as a friend of the veterans, was also hit in the chest by a brick, but was not injured. Two police officers were seriously injured and immediately sent to the hospital. In addition, several police officers and many veterans suffered minor injuries, and many veterans were arrested.

National News Agency, Washington, 28th – The U.S. government authorities have taken decisive action on the long-unresolved veteran relief issue. Yesterday, President Hoover summoned the Secretary of War and the Chief Justice of the Supreme Court, etc., to discuss in detail the legislative and legal issues of evicting these veterans. It seems that the government has decided to take direct action to deal with the situation. Therefore, cavalry, infantry, and tank units were ordered to advance on the veterans stationed in the government offices on Pennsylvania Avenue. The veterans not only refused to withdraw, but also expressed their intention to resist with force. The army then released tear gas into their encampment. The veterans in the buildings could not stay long and scattered. The wind suddenly changed direction, causing hundreds of onlookers to faint. They were all taken to the hospital by the rescue team. When the soldiers fled from the public buildings, fires broke out in many places. It is thought that the soldiers set the fires before leaving, so many people were arrested and will be prosecuted for arson. When the army began to attack the veterans, they were all armed with command swords and bayonets, etc. A large part of the audience were also veterans residing elsewhere, so the cavalry had to try their best to disperse the crowd, sometimes beating the crowd with the backs of their swords. The veterans' weapons were mostly bricks and stones. At that time, someone fired several pistol shots, but it is still unknown if anyone was injured. The person leading the government troops was Chief of Staff MacArthur, who commanded everything on horseback. The casualties in this battle included one death and more than twenty injuries, including three seriously injured. One veteran's ear was cut off by a cavalry command sword. The matter was soon calmed down. General MacArthur declared that he must also evict the residents of the houses in Anacostia Highlands tonight, because there are still about 5,000 men, women, and children who are determined to stay. Afterwards, Walter Waters, the commander of the veterans' departure team, said to the people, "Since this matter was ordered by the President, every drop of blood we shed can be offered under the White House."

National News Agency, Washington, 28th – The veterans have completely withdrawn from Washington tonight, and under the drive of bayonets and machine guns, they have flocked to Baltimore, which is the only way the army left for the veterans to leave the capital. Before the withdrawal, Walter Waters, the commander-in-chief of the veterans' petition group, discussed with the commander of the reception center, Atwell. Waters advocated following the order to withdraw, claiming that it was useless for the veterans to fight against bullets with their bare hands. So the women and children immediately set off, and the men lingered unwilling to leave immediately. When the army arrived, the commander of the reception center, Atwell, alone held a white flag and came out to ask the army commander for an hour's grace, which was granted. The veterans packed up everything and sadly set off at about 10 o'clock at night. Many of the onlookers on the roadside shed tears for them.

Japan's Foreign Trade Import Surplus Exceeds 300 Million

Reuters, Tokyo, July 24 – The Ministry of Finance has now released figures showing that Japan's foreign trade import surplus from January to June this year exceeded 300 million yuan, an increase of about 146 million yuan compared to the import surplus in the same period last year. Although the trade volume this year has increased to 1,445,999,000 yuan (compared to 1,331,805,000 yuan in the same period last year), exports have decreased by about 20.5 million yuan. Statistics for the past six months show that the total value of exports was 572,583,000 yuan, while the same period last year was 593,015,000 yuan. This year's imports totaled 873,416,000 yuan, compared to 738,790,000 yuan in the same period last year. Specifically for the month of June, this year's import surplus was 17,333,000 yuan, while last year's import surplus for this month was only 9,980,000 yuan. In the past six months, Japan's cash exports totaled 79,102,000 yuan, while cash imports were only 810,000 yuan. In comparison, the cash export surplus reached 78,292,000 yuan, which is the opposite of last year's situation, as the cash import surplus in the same period last year was 7,520,000 yuan. There are more than a dozen types of foreign goods with increased imports this year, with raw materials being the most significant. From January to May, the import of raw cotton was worth 251,455,000 yuan, compared to 166,889,000 yuan in the same period last year. The import of iron plates was approximately double that of the previous year, and the import of aluminum was approximately seven times higher than last year. In the past five months, the Japanese goods with increased exports were primarily cotton yarn, which increased approximately three times, as well as rayon. The export of rayon textiles increased by approximately four million yuan.

Recent News on the Communist Case in Ningxiang, Hunan Province

Central Investigation Committee Has Arrived in Hunan

The Clearing Department Announces the Course of the Case

Changsha Correspondence – After the Communist case in Ningxiang, Hunan Province, occurred, the provincial Party and government authorities attached great importance to it and repeatedly reported it to the Central Government, requesting that senior officials be sent to Hunan to thoroughly investigate the case. The Central Government also considered the case to be of great importance and sent Committee Member Fang Juehui and Committee Member Hong Ludong to Hunan. The two committee members, Fang and Hong, arrived in the province by express train on the morning of the 20th at 9:00 a.m. After getting off the train, they went to the Youth Association to rest with Chairman He and others. They immediately began actively collecting the case files and have now transferred and stored the various case files of the Provincial Party Department's Clearing Department regarding this case for review, hoping to appropriately resolve the case as soon as possible. As for the details of the case's occurrence and the Clearing Department's handling process, the Clearing Command announced the details yesterday, the text of which is quite lengthy and recorded as follows:

The Past Bandit Situation in Ningxiang – Investigation shows that Ningxiang is the birthplace of the main Red bandits Xie Juecai, He Shuheng, Wang Lingbo, etc. The Red bandits have had organizations there for a long time. After the Ma-Ri Incident, more than 700 Red bandits in the county declared their surrender, many of whom pretended to surrender and secretly worked in various sectors. In addition, the local bandit leaders Yan Ruoqiao, Xu Shangda, Zhong Jie, Cai Zhengbiao, etc., organized the Central Hunan Pseudo-Guerrilla Team, which disturbed the area and greatly affected the province's security. Moreover, the county's Party Department had a complex internal structure and repeatedly published statements against the Central and local governments. It also colluded with former county magistrate Li Jiapu and former Security Brigade Commander Wu Dongcheng under the guise of appeasement, which strengthened the bandit forces, leading to frequent incidents of robbing guns from various township bureaus. (Investigation reveals that the Tongwen Town and Gaolu Township bureaus suffered heavy losses. According to a report by former Brigade Commander Wu Dongcheng, the Gaolu Bureau was robbed by bandits of 16 rifles, 1 Mauser pistol, 1 square pistol, more than 100 rounds of ammunition, 1 generator, 22 sets of military uniforms, and all symbol flags, etc. The Tong Bureau was robbed by bandits of 24 rifles, 4 pistols, more than 800 rounds of ammunition, etc. None of the bureaus resisted, and the bandits only numbered about 20 each time they robbed the bureaus' guns, and they only carried a few guns and sticks. A small number of bandits robbed a large number of guns, etc.) ○ Seeing this situation, the Clearing Command reorganized the county's Security Brigade and established the Yiyang, Xiangxiang, Ningxiang, and Anhua Bandit Suppression Command to jointly encircle and suppress the bandits, in order to achieve a thorough suppression.

Clues to Uncovering the Case – Investigation shows that on May 4 this year, the Public Security Bureau of the Hunan Provincial Capital cracked the Wang Wu case of the Pseudo-Changsha Municipal Committee and found many Red bandit plots and secret notices in its organization. Among them was a notice directing the work of the Pseudo-Guerrilla Team, stating that its main task was to assist in the riots of its people, and that the Guerrilla Team must use these materials to publicize and agitate on various revolutionary anniversaries and special events, such as the current anti-Japanese and flood disasters. Because the suspect was stubborn and unwilling to confess the details, he was executed according to the law. Subsequently, the Red bandit wanted criminal Mei Chongdong, also known as Mei Zhongdong, was arrested in Xiangtan, and a pistol, ammunition, and evidence of extortion were seized on the spot. After the Clearing Command brought him to trial, he confessed that he was the commander of the Pseudo-Guerrilla Team and, like the executed bandit leader Wang Wu, had received a mission from the Pseudo-Central Committee to come to Hunan. He knew the Red bandit organization situation in the county quite well and had the potential to solve the case. Therefore, members of the special service team were ordered to escort him to Ningxiang County to search for bandit guns and arrest the remaining members, and the Ningxiang County government and Security Brigade were ordered to assist at any time.

Progress After Uncovering the Pseudo-Organization – After the special service team members escorted the bandit suspect to Ningxiang, they uncovered the Pseudo-County Committee organization in Shaohu Xinwu and arrested a Pseudo-County Committee member, Xiao Meiyu.

Then, the bandits Yang Baosheng, Yang Shousheng, Xiao Jinghai, Chen Shulin, Wang Bangheng, etc., were arrested one after another. In the Youzhayuan Primary School in Tongwen Town, where the surrendered Communist Party member Chen Yuchu was the speaker, 7 rifles and 699 rounds of ammunition were seized. According to the confession of the Pseudo-

He also confessed that the pseudo-guerrilla members in Ningxiang mostly lived in the Xiaowumen Machang area. Most of the communists in the provincial capital were cart drivers, power plant workers and spinning mill workers. They held meetings in the mountains in the suburbs and on boats on the water and on Tianxin Pavilion Ring City Road, etc. Based on this investigation, the Red Bandits' offensive in Hunan is actually an entire scheme, and the central Hunan barrier province, especially the provincial capital, is very important. If it is brewed for a long time, then the disease will be born from the armpit, and the hidden dangers will be more serious.

Marine Corps Relieved by Guards Brigade After Leaving Qiong

Chen Zhangfu Concurrently Appointed Pacification Commissioner of Qiongya

Guangzhou dispatch: Following Cai Tingkai's mediation of the Qiong affair, the 19th Route Army's Brigade Commander Tan Qixiu was dispatched to Qiong to handle the transfer of defenses between the two sides. Chen Ce's Marine Corps was originally scheduled to leave Qiong as soon as possible. However, due to the delayed arrival of the merchant ships "Hai Shun" and "Guang Li," which were chartered to Qiong to transport troops, and the insufficient allocation of ships, the departure was postponed until the 20th of this month. Only one battalion was left behind to withdraw after the relieving troops arrived. According to Tan Qixiu's telegram late on the 20th, Chen Jitang's directly subordinate Guards Brigade from Leizhou had arrived on Qiong Island on the night of the 20th. The Marine Corps completely departed for Xiamen on the morning of the 21st. Furthermore, Chen Hanguang, the Guards Brigade Commander, telegraphed at 7 PM on the afternoon of the 20th, stating that the advance troops of his brigade would arrive at Dongshui Port that night and proceed to the old city of Chengmai to camp. Tan Qixiu, having completed the procedures for the Marine Corps, returned to the provincial capital during the day to report the progress to Chen Jitang, and then proceeded to Fujian Province to preside over military affairs. Upon investigation, He Baoshu's detachment, the second regiment of Chen Hanguang's Brigade advance troops, arrived in Haikou on the afternoon of the 20th, and was subsequently ordered to proceed to Qiongdong, Wenchang, and Jiaji to be stationed. After the remaining units, Chen Hanguang's first regiment and Peng Zhifang's third regiment, arrived in Qiong, Chen's regiment was stationed in Lingao and Chengmai, and Peng's regiment was stationed in Ganen, Lingshui, and Yaxian. The special service battalion and brigade headquarters were stationed in Qiongzhou Prefecture city. As for the issue of governance in Qiongya, the current intention of the Guangdong authorities is to establish a Qiongya Pacification Commissioner's Office in Qiong, under the command and supervision of the First Army Group and the provincial government. It has already been internally decided that Chen Zhangfu will concurrently serve as Commissioner of the Qiongya Pacification Office. As Qiongya borders the Southern District, having Chen manage the Qiong affairs will facilitate measures. Chen has already been ordered to dispatch personnel to Qiong to prepare for the establishment of the Pacification Commissioner's Office, and he himself will personally proceed to Qiongzhou from Leizhou within days to make arrangements. It is rumored that the Qiongya Pacification Office will be established on August 1st. Furthermore, at the provincial affairs meeting on the 21st, the Department of Civil Affairs proposed to appoint a new batch of county magistrates for Qiongya. The county magistrates for Qiongdong County, Qiongshan County, Chengmai County, Dingan County, Wanning County, and Changjiang County have already been approved for replacement. These newly appointed county magistrates have been ordered to proceed to take office immediately. In view of this, since the Qiongya Pacification Office has already been established and the Department of Civil Affairs has also appointed new county magistrates for the various counties of Qiongya, the so-called Qiongya Special District system has been implicitly abolished. Wu Chaochu, the Chief Executive of the Qiongya Special District, sent a letter to Chen Jitang some time ago, but Chen has not yet replied. Yesterday, a certain senior official was dispatched to Hong Kong to communicate with Wu on all matters. Wu intends to go north with Chen Ce during the day. The Qiongya Special District has, in fact, been abolished, and the Southern Route issue, which has been a source of disturbance for over a month, has thus been completely resolved. (July 23rd)

Recent Developments in the Suppression of Bandits in Southern Jiangxi

Northeast Jiang Area Tightens Security

Southern Jiangxi's Defenses are Very Solid

Yu Hanmou Commands Troops from Three Provinces

Guangzhou dispatch: Since the Communist bandits in southern Jiangxi retreated to Xinfeng, the military leaders of northern Guangdong have concentrated in Nanxiong. Chen Jitang specially dispatched Li Yangjing, the Commander of the Third Army, to Xiong some time ago to discuss future plans for pursuing and suppressing the Communist bandits and coordinating with friendly forces with the military leaders. After the meeting in Xiong, Li returned to the provincial capital to report to Chen Jitang. Chen Jitang then convened a military conference at headquarters at 9 AM on the 23rd to discuss the strategy for pursuing and suppressing the Communist bandits. Li Yangjing reported on the discussions with the military leaders in Shaozhou and Nanxiong. Subsequently, the senior military officers made detailed discussions and resolved many military plans, which were telegraphed to the front-line generals for implementation that day. Regarding the recent military situation at the front, although there are no bandit traces in the Nanxiong area, it is rumored that local communists infiltrated Qiannan from Xiaojiangkou, Longnan, on the 21st of the month, with a force of about 10,000 people, dividing to harass Longxianxu and Nanpu, which are part of Wengyuan County, on the Guangdong border. Longxianxu is located ninety-five li west of Wengyuan County seat, while Nanpu is located more than one hundred li east of the county seat. If these places are alarmed, the defenses of Lianping and Heping in East Jiang and Wengyuan and Yingde in North Jiang will simultaneously be strained. Therefore, after discovering the alarming news from Longxian on the morning of the 21st, Hao, the magistrate of Wengyuan County, immediately sent a special envoy to Wangfu Gang and telegraphed the Northwest District Pacification Headquarters in Shaoguan to request assistance. Upon receiving the report, Li Han魂 first dispatched Gui Army Commander Wang Zanbin's division to Yingde to await orders, and also ordered Li Gang, the Deputy Commander of the Third Independent Division, to lead the third regiment of the division, commanded by Qiu Guisheng, to return from Nanxiong to Hetou, Yingde, and then proceed to Wangfu Gang and Wengyuan to suppress and intercept the bandits as opportunities arise. At the same time, the First Army Group Headquarters telegraphed Li Zhenliang's regiment of the Second Army's Fifth Division and Huang Zhiwen's detachment of the Third Army's Eighth Division, which were stationed in Laolong, to intensify their vigilance in Lianping and Heping to prevent the Communist bandits from Longxian from infiltrating east. As for the Third Army's Seventh Division, it took over the defense of Meixian, while Huang Renhuan's detachment of the Second Independent Division returned to Pingyuan and Jiaoling to guard the area around Xunwu and Baichi. This is the current situation of the Guangdong army's defense of the Northeast Jiang area. As for Southern Jiangxi, from Nan'an downwards, the Guangdong army is still maintaining a strong defense. From Meiling upwards, Dayu to Nankang and Ganzhou, Yu Hanmou's troops and the Central Army are continuously increasing troops and deploying defenses. Recently, two more divisions of the Xiang Army, commanded by Wang Dongyuan and Chen Guangzhong, have arrived, making the defense even more solid. After entering western Jiangxi, Wang and Chen's divisions advanced towards Shangyou, defeating Li Mingrui's Communist bandit force in Shangyou. They then advanced to Yingqian to search and suppress bandits. They have now established contact with Yu Hanmou's troops and Chen Cheng's troops. Recently, Chairman Chiang has ordered Liu Jianxu, the commander of the Xiang Army, to assemble the majority of his troops and advance rapidly from Yingqian to Nankang and Dayu. All of Yu Hanmou's two divisions (Li and Ye), Chen Cheng's two divisions (Zhou and Li), Liu Jianxu's two divisions (Wang and Chen), and Ma Kun's brigade in Southern Jiangxi are under the command and deployment of Army Commander Yu Hanmou to unify orders. (July 25th)

The Tiger Plague in Henan is Almost Throughout the Province

Requests for Medicine from Various Places Come in an Endless Stream

Kaifeng dispatch: Reports of tiger plague and requests for medicine from various counties in Henan Province have reached more than thirty counties. The speed of transmission, the severity of the damage, and the number of deaths are generally similar, as has been disclosed in previous reports. At the moment, reports of plague and requests for medicine from various places continue to pour in, an endless stream. The trend is almost throughout the entire province. A brief description follows:

Yu Xunduo, the magistrate of Luyi County, stated in a telegram on the 17th: "The tiger plague in Bozhou is rampant, with vomiting and diarrhea leading to death within two to three hours, making rescue impossible. It has now spread to the eastern border of our county, with twenty to thirty deaths per day. In addition to supervising the Public Security Bureau to do their utmost to prevent and control the epidemic, I earnestly request your association to quickly provide medicine for rescue, to avoid delaying the people's livelihood."

He Xuehai, the magistrate of Xuchang County, stated in a telegram on the 19th: "The survivors of the disaster in our county are now suffering from a seasonal epidemic. Cholera is rampant among the residents of the city and countryside. In the past ten days, the number of deaths has been in the hundreds, especially among hawkers and laborers, who are suffering from the severe heat during the day and sleeping in the open at night. The transmission is rapid and extremely dangerous. In addition to supervising the Public Security Bureau to do our utmost to prevent it, I earnestly request the rapid distribution of a large quantity of medicines for rescue."

Sun Hongling, the magistrate of Queshan County, stated in a telegram on the 19th: "The tiger plague in our county is rampant, with twenty to thirty deaths in the city every day. Vomiting, diarrhea, and abdominal pain lead to immediate death. The spread is widening daily, and the situation is extremely dangerous. Please quickly provide a large quantity of medicine for rescue, as the need is extremely urgent."

Brief News

At the behest of the order, the county magistrate also stated in a letter: "The tiger plague is raging in the cities and villages of this county. Malaria, dysentery, heatstroke, and fever are everywhere. Recently, the tiger plague has also occurred, with dozens of deaths per day. Often, entire families are infected and die one after another. The poor survivors of the disaster are unable to save themselves and are waiting to die, a truly pitiful situation. Xinan County: Relief sub-committee's Shao Huiguang reported: "This county is suffering from severe drought and extreme heat in the summer, resulting in plague and cholera occurring everywhere. Seven or eight out of ten people in the villages are infected with this disease and die within days without receiving treatment. Only Jisheng Water, Ten-Drop Water, Wanying Jizhong Water, Wolong Pills and other medicines are still effective. We earnestly request your esteemed association to issue various medicines to facilitate rescue."

Guo Fangwu of the Yiluo River Works Office telegraphed on the 24th: "Mr. Du Senlin brought medicine to Luo and distributed it to the Luozhen Society's epidemic prevention department and to various construction sites under our office. In recent days, the tiger plague in Luo, Yan, and Mengjin counties has become more severe, with hundreds of deaths per day, especially among the workers affected by the disaster. Several foremen have died, causing panic among the people. It is hoped that a doctor will be dispatched quickly with medicine to provide treatment and prevent the spread."

The Closing of the National Postal Union Conference

The National Postal Workers' Union held its fourth plenary session on the afternoon of the 27th, with 48 representatives in attendance, chaired by Yang Zonglian. The discussion items were: (1) The meeting place of local unions should be located inside the post office. If there is no spare room in the bureau, the bureau should subsidize the rent of the meeting place. The resolution was to pass it in principle and submit it to the ministry for consideration of the local situation and allocate meeting places or subsidize rent. (2) Yang Fu, Li Jinghan, the executive committee members of the former Beiping Postal Workers' Union, were unfairly dismissed for their efforts in union affairs. The resolution was to pass it in principle and request the authorities to approve their reinstatement. A letter was sent to the transportation authorities in the name of the conference to approve their reinstatement and handed over to the preparatory committee of the general union for handling negotiations. (3) Please strive to have the government promulgate special union laws as soon as possible or separate regulations for the organization of postal unions to facilitate the postal workers' movement and increase the strength of the national revolution. The resolution was to pass it in principle. The measures were: (1) Strive to request the central party headquarters to promulgate special union laws as soon as possible or separate regulations for the organization of postal unions, based on the draft special union law drafted by the preparatory committee of the National Postal Workers' Union. (2) When discussing the separate regulations for postal unions, the Central Government is requested to allow the postal union to send representatives to attend and provide reference opinions. (3) Send representatives to petition the Central Government. (4) Improve the treatment of letter carriers, postmen, handymen, coolies, sailors, etc. The resolution was to pass it in principle. According to the opinions of the original proposers, the following measures were decided to be recommended to the ministry for approval: (1) Determine and increase the salaries of letter carriers and lower levels. (2) Issue winter uniforms to letter carriers and postmen. (3) Letter carriers and lower-level workers should enjoy long vacation benefits. (4) Solicitous messengers should receive the same treatment as letter carriers, and the name should be changed to letter carrier. (5) Temporary workers should be changed to formal coolies. (6) Inland errand boys should be changed to extra errand runners and receive the same treatment as Shanghai extra errand runners. (7) Stipulate the duties of mail errand runners and official errand runners. (8) For letter carriers and lower levels, screening examinations should be stipulated and preferential treatment should be given. (9) Letter carriers should be uniformly issued leather shoes, socks, and leather bags. (10) Stipulate the date of rest for errand runners and provide appropriate food and lodging allowances. (11) Issue errand runner coolies with leather shoes. (12) Inland letter carriers should receive the same treatment as the administration bureau letter carriers. (13) Errand runners should receive the same treatment as letter carriers. (14) New uniforms should be uniformly issued to letter carriers and postmen in second- and third-class post offices across the country. (5) Popularize education for postal workers and their children. The resolution was to pass it in principle. The measures decided to be submitted to the ministry for approval were: (1) Run schools for postal workers' children in various places. If primary schools have already been run, junior high schools should be run quickly. (2) Vocational training classes should be widely established in various places. (3) Libraries and postal worker academic research classes should be established in various places. (6) Improve vacation time. The resolution was to pass it in principle. The measures decided were as follows, suggesting that the authorities implement them: A. Long vacation (1) If leave is not approved when due, full salary should be issued separately. (2) Reserve personnel should be increased and leave should be approved on schedule without delay to avoid being a "hollow benefit". B. Short vacation (1) It should not be postponed without reason. (2) Every January, those who have not applied for leave or whose leave has not been approved or partially approved within a year should be calculated and given full salary for the unannounced vacation time to show encouragement. C. Regular holiday All levels of employees should rest on all regular holidays. D. Sick leave should not be hindered, deducted, or delayed. E. Special leave Restore one week of summer vacation. F. All levels of employees should enjoy the same treatment for all types of leave. The meeting adjourned at 6 PM.

The National Detached-Area Postal Workers' Union held its fifth meeting at 9:00 a.m. on the 28th with the attendance of more than 50 representatives from various areas. Key points of cases passed: (1) Formulate an anti-Japanese work plan and hand it over to the General Labor Union to formulate a concrete plan and issue a circular to all local unions for earnest compliance. (2) The Postal Administration's Circular No. 904 stipulates the modification of the methods for achievement examination, testing and selection. (3) Suggest to the authorities that the lower levels of letter carriers and all levels of workers be upgraded by one level. (4) Suggest to the authorities the construction of postal worker dormitories. (5) The following cases, after review, are proposed to be handled by the Preparatory Committee and submitted to the Congress for public resolution. A. Regarding the proposals of the Bureau, there are 28 cases, such as cases in which all mail must be transported by car in places where trains and machines are already running, and crackdowns on private transportation of mail. B. Regarding union affairs, there are 17 cases, such as the authorities deducting union dues on behalf of the union. C. Regarding welfare, there are 30 cases, such as the unconstrained allowance of the management bureau. D. The following cases are proposed to be submitted to the Preparatory Committee for reference and appropriate handling, and should be resolved by the Congress. (1) The authorities shall not be jealous of employees and reduce their grades. (2) Local unions should publish publications. (3) Free mailing of union mail. (4) Local unions may send special agents to inspect the diligence and laziness of postal inspectors. (5) When postal workers upgrade every three years, they should still be members of this union. The National Postal Workers' Conference held its closing ceremony as scheduled on the afternoon of the 28th. Forty-five representatives attended, and Wang Shufan was the chairman. The ceremony was carried out as usual. The chairman reported on the progress of the conference and thanked all the representatives for their guidance. Later, Xu Wentian, the representative of the Central Government, Zhang Yaode, the representative of the National Government, and Zhou Bomin, the representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, delivered speeches. After the chairman's reply, the meeting was adjourned with slogans. At 4:00 p.m., all the representatives, led by Xu Wentian, sent by the Central Government, took twelve cars to worship at the tomb of the Prime Minister and presented two wreaths. They then visited the Martyrs' Cemetery and the Central Sports Field in Linggu Temple, and returned to the city at 6:00 p.m.

The Economic Crisis in Rural Anhui

Abundant Harvest of Rice, Surplus Grain, Market Prices Plummet

Wuhu dispatch: Among China's agricultural products, Anhui ranks as an important rice producer. In prosperous years, the rice from various counties in southern Anhui would gather at Wuhu Port, and exports would reach over 9 million shi. Although there was a major flood last year, there was still a surplus of about 3 million shi of rice that was successively exported. This year, due to the timely rainfall and the recovery of the rice paddies from last year's disaster, the soil is even more fertile, and the grain yield is twice as high as in previous years. Before the new rice has even appeared on the market, rice prices have already plummeted. In the span of a month, the price has dropped from 11 yuan per dan to about 6.5 yuan. Underproduction leading to insufficient consumption is a cause for poverty, but overproduction exceeding consumption is even more dangerous. After the disaster, farmers pawned possessions and took out loans to maintain their livelihoods and barely continue farming. All their hopes are pinned on the autumn harvest. Based on the predicted grain prices, the price of new rice may not exceed 2.5 yuan per shi, and the rice price will only be about 5 yuan. Farmers who borrowed one shi of rice last year must now repay four shi of rice. There is a hidden worry of bankruptcy in rural areas. In recent days, the rice ears, due to their weight, have been hanging down to the ground. Farmers are deeply afraid of the rice germinating due to flooding, and are already rushing to harvest day and night. (July 26th)

Local Dispatches

Changshu

Meat Ticket Escapes by Seizing Opportunity: Sun Jinsheng and his son, who run a tofu shop in Chengbeixiang, Fifteenth District, were kidnapped by bandits on the morning of the 17th of this month at 3 AM. After the village chief reported the incident to the District Office, the District Office and the Public Security Bureau requested the county government to find a way to rescue them. The next day, Sun Jinsheng's son was sent by the bandits to Xitangqian and instructed to prepare 3,000 yuan quickly and go to Da'anjiang in Jiangbei to redeem his father. The family was extremely anxious because they did not have this huge sum of money. Unexpectedly, Jinsheng suddenly returned home safely the day before yesterday (the 26th). According to his own account, after being kidnapped, he was taken by boat to Da'anjiang and was repeatedly beaten severely, suffering greatly. Fortunately, the bandit leader suddenly suffered a severe attack of cholera the night before, and the remaining bandits tried their best to rescue him. By dawn, all the bandits were extremely tired and sound asleep, so he seized the opportunity to sneak ashore and escape to Niuhongdichu, where he took a boat to Shanghai and returned home by a roundabout route.

Watermelon Boat Robbed Midway: At midnight on the 27th, a watermelon boat, loaded with watermelons from Xihugangkou, was heading to the city to sell them. When passing the Hqiao outside the West Gate, it suddenly encountered a bandit boat coming head-on. As it approached the watermelon boat, more than a dozen strong men, wielding knives and sticks, swarmed onto the boat, tied up the two crew members and beat them violently, forcing them to reveal where they had hidden the money. After searching repeatedly, they found nothing and transported all the watermelons and clothes on board to their own boat and sped away.

Wuxi

Village Woman Beaten to Death and Body Abandoned in River: Gu Afu, a villager in Nanqianxiang, Eleventh District (Nanyan City), which is under the jurisdiction of the county, has been guarding the Zhou family's ancestral hall and farming for a living. His wife, Wang, 26 years old, was returning to Ning on the morning of the 20th of this month. While passing through the Susheqiao area, she rested in the shade of a tree because of the hot weather. She happened to see a melon field nearby with fragrant melons, so she picked two and ate them. Unexpectedly, Wang Zhugenquan (nicknamed "Pockmarked Genquan") of the melon field saw her. Without asking for an explanation, he beat Wang severely with a carrying pole. She soon died of her injuries. Seeing that he had caused a disaster, Genquan threw the body into the river at that place in an attempt to destroy the evidence. Afterwards, Zhang Sannan, the head of the 396th Tu, reported to Afu, the deceased's husband, that his wife had accidentally fallen into the river and drowned while washing peaches at the Susheqiao riverside. Upon hearing this, Afu rushed to the scene, retrieved the body, and hurriedly put it in a coffin. At the same time, he reported to the District Office of the district, who forwarded it to the county government, requesting justice. However, the murderer, Zhu Genquan, had already heard the news and fled, and his whereabouts are unknown.

Boatman Becomes Rich Overnight and Searched by Police: The area under Yingxiu Bridge inside the West Gate of this county is where Jiangbei Peng households gather, and they usually make a living by collecting garbage and working as small vendors. The other day, a young fellow villager from Jiangbei, wearing fancy clothes, suddenly arrived at the home of boatman Liu Erlang, carrying more than 2,000 yuan in banknotes. He claimed to be a manager at a certain foreign company in Shanghai and bought a Xiangyusha shirt as a gift for Liu's daughter. The boatman wearing fancy clothes aroused suspicion, and someone secretly reported it to the Public Security First Branch, which sent police to search the boat. More than 300 yuan in banknotes and a pawn ticket were found in the rice bucket. When asked about it, Liu Erlang claimed that the young man was his nephew, who was doing business in Shanghai and had now returned to Shanghai. Director Gao of the branch obtained the confession and ordered Liu Erlang to post bail and have his nephew go to the branch to claim it within ten days, otherwise the banknotes would be confiscated.

Changzhou

Disbanding of Wounded and Sick Soldiers: The Wuyi Temporary Clearance Committee for Wounded and Sick Soldiers, following the orders of the Military Commission, has been sorting out the wounded and sick soldiers who have recovered from various hospitals in recent days, assigning them to return to their units or disbanding them, and ordering them to leave the country within a certain time limit. Those who have not recovered will still be treated by the respective hospitals, and they are strictly prohibited from going out to avoid causing trouble. However, it has recently been discovered that some of the wounded and sick soldiers who have been assigned to return to their units and given severance pay are still lingering in the country under various pretexts. A letter has been sent to the First Battalion of the First Regiment of the Changzhou Garrison to arrest them at any time. The battalion believes that this matter is of great concern to local security and has specially announced that if they continue to linger in this county, once they are found, regardless of whether they have committed a crime or not, they will all be charged with obstructing public security as bad elements.

Zhenjiang

Collapse of Jiang'an, Liuhaokou: The Jiang'an in front of the motor vehicle terminal at Liuhaokou, across the river from this port, has collapsed by more than twenty zhang due to the strong east wind and the white waves that have turned silver in recent days. The neighborhood is alarmed. The ferry for the cars has been changed to the Puji Terminal and travelers must walk half a li.

Yangzhou

End of Flood Relief Association: At nine in the morning on the 28th, the Jiangdu County Flood Relief Association held a joint meeting of executive and supervisory committees to discuss the closing matters. Wang Hanfu, Gong Kuishi and other seventeen people attended. Wang Jingting, the chairman, reported a rough income statement of over nine thousand yuan, with five thousand yuan in expenses. (2) It was resolved to allocate 1,000 yuan to Ba District for relief. (3) It was resolved that the remaining money would be deposited in the Bank of China and Wang Jingting, Hu Yanbo, Dai Tianqiu, Liu Zikun and Yang Shengwu would be responsible for safekeeping. In case of disaster, the executive supervisory committee would convene and resolve to use it. (4) A decision was made to compile and print a testimonial and publish the work income and expenditure in the newspaper. (rest omitted)

Sudden Downpour After Long Drought: This year's summer has been extremely dry. Not only has the tiger epidemic been rampant in the Jiangbei area, but the rice in the mountain fields and dams has also been severely wilted. There were worries that there would be no hope for the autumn harvest and that disasters would occur frequently. However, yesterday (the 26th) at two o'clock in the afternoon, the sky suddenly became gloomy and dark, and a heavy rain poured down. Although the time was too short, such a timely rain could save the long-parched fields and alleviate all epidemics.

Gaoyou

Zhangjia Village Repeatedly Robbed Four Families: More than ten bandits armed with guns suddenly arrived at Zhangjia Village, District 5 under the county, the night before last. They divided into groups and robbed Rong Taichang Grocery Store, Dequan Tea Shop, and the homes of farmers such as Tian Baowan, and others, for three hours before leaving with the stolen goods. It is said that the losses amounted to more than two thousand yuan.

Pig Boat Capsizes, Rescued: On the 11th District of the county, at Songjia Bridge, around 1:00 PM the day before yesterday, a villager named Zhu Hongwan loaded a boat with over thirty pigs, planning to sell them in Yang. Unexpectedly, when they reached the Jiujing Lake entrance, they encountered a sudden strong wind and huge waves, which overturned the boat. The "Ji" character marked red boat saw this and immediately rushed to rescue them. They rescued seven people and over thirty pigs from Zhu Hongwan's boat, and they were fortunate to survive.

Hurricane Destroys Houses and Injures People: In this county today (26th), around 3:00 PM, dark clouds suddenly gathered, accompanied by thunder and heavy rain, followed by a hurricane. Although it lasted only a short time, the losses were quite extensive. The investigation is as follows: In the backyard of Wu Xiaojia, a merchant in the Huaidequan Alley in the central market of the city, there was a locust tree that was over a hundred years old. When the wind rose, it snapped the tree in half and destroyed one of Wu Xiaojia's thatched houses, and also destroyed two bedrooms and two guest rooms in the house of pharmacist Tao Yunqing. At that time, Tao Yunqing happened to be sleeping in the room and was injured in the head by bricks and tiles. Fortunately, the injuries were not serious and there was no major problem. However, the appliances and displays in the bedrooms and guest rooms were severely damaged, and the loss is said to be quite large. In addition, the ancient Sanyuan Hall temple on Gaogong Bridge in the city, which was built during the Ming Dynasty, had its roof ridge destroyed by the hurricane. Furthermore, numerous thatched houses outside the North Gate and on the Yun Causeway, as well as awnings in the streets, were destroyed by the hurricane.

Two Cases of Robbery by Water and Land: Fisherman Zhou Changlong, who now runs a rice business, went to Cheluo Town the day before yesterday to sell rice, obtaining 160 silver dollars and 4,000 cash coins. He set sail for Huxi, but unexpectedly, when they reached the Xinhe area of the 11th District, they encountered a bandit boat with four bandits jumping out, each wielding guns. Under the guise of inspection, they robbed the boat of all its money and silver. Furthermore, at the home of Xu Anbo, a resident near Dongdun Town in the county, more than ten bandits suddenly arrived the night before last, each armed with guns. They broke down the door and entered, robbing for several hours before leaving at dawn, with a loss of three to four hundred yuan.

Pinghu

A Glimpse of the Rampant Epidemic: In the past ten days, the epidemic has not subsided. More than ten residents in the city and suburbs die from the disease every day. The spread in the countryside is also rapid. The wife of Qi Rongxian in Xishi of Xincang Town, someone from the staff of Shi Shunxing's dowry shop in Dongshi, an elderly woman surnamed Ma in Diyu Township, a student partner of Xi Wanxiang, Zhu Fujin of the porter class, Zhang Xian of Cangji Street, and a family of four in Qianjia Yi Road have all died from cholera. The number of deaths in the countryside is countless. From this, we can see a glimpse of the rampant epidemic.

Melon Vendor Falls into River and Drowns: Zhang Fuchang, a farmer from the north and south sand area of ​​Sigu Bridge, along with three companions, loaded watermelons to sell in Songjiang. After selling them, they were towed back to Ping by the Hongni Ban steamship with an empty boat. At 3:00 AM yesterday morning, when they arrived at Lugong Bridge outside the East Gate of this city, because the bridge opening was narrow and too many boats were being towed, the boat hit the bridge pier with a loud crash. Zhang was shocked and fell into the river. The wheel knew it had caused the disaster and tried harder to rescue him, but it was too late.

Taizhou

Woman Commits Suicide by Swallowing Opium: A woman named Yu Wang in the west of Linhai City, due to an argument with her stepson at 2:00 PM today (25th), suddenly had a suicidal thought and swallowed raw opium to kill herself. After being noticed by her family, they hired a doctor from Pujiyiyuan, but it was too late, and she died shortly after.

Educational News Highlights

President Li Zheng of Beijing Normal University Comes to Beijing

Requests Flexibility Regarding Suspension of Enrollment

Meets to Discuss the Direction of Reorganizing Normal University

The previous student unrest at Beijing Normal University was due to factional divisions among the students. They nominated three candidates for president and requested the government to appoint one. In fact, none of the three nominated could come, and the government was unlikely to approve the request. This was because a small number of students were taking advantage of the lack of a president to act freely, while the majority of students were dissatisfied with the selfishness of the minority and had blockaded the student union. As a result, the students were at odds with each other, and the school was unstable. After Li Zheng arrived at the school, he explained and persuaded them in various ways, unsealing the student union so that students could operate within the proper framework. If anything went beyond the scope, the administrative authorities would stop and punish it. The small number of students who first started the trouble have been safely taken care of due to the general trend. Now the school is calm, and the deans of each college and the heads of each department have been appointed (referring to the existing professors). Preparations are being made to start enrollment, but since the Ministry of Education ordered the suspension of enrollment, the school has felt difficult. President Li arrived in Beijing on the 28th to negotiate with the Ministry of Education, requesting flexibility regarding the suspension of enrollment at Beijing Normal University. Minister Zhu believed that this matter was related to the government's entire reorganization plan and did not give a definite answer. President Li met with Minister Zhu to discuss the direction of reorganizing Beijing Normal University's education. It is said that he will stay in Beijing for several days, waiting for the matter to be completed before returning to Ping.

Local News

Jinan Students Actively Protect the School

Yesterday Visited School Director Wu Tiecheng

| School Will Move Back to Zhenru Tomorrow |

The Jinan University student body's school protection movement, in addition to sending representatives to Beijing to petition the Executive Yuan's Ministry of Education to strongly request the revocation of the order and convening major middle schools in the city to request assistance to expand the organization and strengthen its forces to achieve its goal, has recently requested the school directors to come forward to help. The Guangdong school directors in Beijing have successively sent telegrams requesting it. Yesterday, they also visited the school directors Kong Yongzhi and Wu Tiecheng in Shanghai. Director Wu received them at the Municipal Government at 10:00 AM yesterday. The representatives of the school protection association, Tao Yi and Zhu Dunli, first reported the significance and process of this school protection. Next, they expressed their hopes and requests to Director Kong. Director Wu greatly appreciated the school protection enthusiasm and the reasons for protecting the school, and agreed to go to Beijing in one or two days to lobby the government authorities, requesting the revocation of the order so that the matter would not escalate and be resolved as soon as possible.

Furthermore, it is reported that Jinan University, which was previously damaged in the Shanghai Incident, rented a house on Hart Road, and half a semester has passed since the start of the school year. Now, due to the end of the school year, it plans to move back to Zhenru immediately. The school held a relocation meeting at 1:00 PM the day before yesterday, chaired by Secretary Zheng Baoning, and decided to move back to the original school in Zhenru on July 31.

National Sports Conference

| Rules for Attending |

Rules for Reviewing Proposals

The National Sports Conference is scheduled to be held in Beijing starting on August 16. The recently formulated rules for attending and reviewing proposals are recorded below:

Rules for Attending the National Sports Conference

Article 1: The National Sports Conference attendance tickets are divided into two types: single-use and long-term use.

Article 2: All educational academic institutions or groups, newspapers, and news agencies in Beijing and abroad that have been recognized by the Ministry of Education may submit a formal letter to the Preparatory Committee in advance to request the issuance of long-term attendance tickets, limited to two people per institution and group.

Article 3: Staff members of institutions, students of schools, and members of groups who are enthusiastic about sports may obtain proof from their respective institutions and groups to request the issuance of single-use attendance tickets.

Article 4: The validity period of a single-use attendance ticket is limited to the day, and the validity period of a long-term attendance ticket is the same as the conference period, but the number of tickets is fixed. If they have been issued, further requests may be rejected.

Article 5: For the attendance tickets issued to various institutions, groups, newspapers, and news agencies, the name of the institution, etc., and the name of the representative must be written on the ticket.

Article 6: When attending the venue, attendees must hand over the attendance ticket to the ticket inspector for inspection. Those without a ticket or with a ticket that is soiled and cannot be identified will not be allowed to enter.

Article 7: Attendees must sign the attendee registration book when entering the venue.

Article 8: News reporters must obtain a news reporter badge from the Preparatory Committee before entering the specially designated news reporter seat.

Article 9: Attendees must abide by the order of the venue. If any of the following circumstances occur, the chairman may order them to leave or cancel their attendance ticket at his discretion: (1) carrying items that are not needed for the venue; (2) expressing approval or disapproval of the members' speeches or chatting with each other; (3) leaving the attendee seat without authorization, disrupting the order of the venue.

Article 10: If attendees have printed materials or souvenirs to send to members, they should hand them over to the Preparatory Committee to distribute them on their behalf as appropriate.

Article 11: These rules shall be implemented after being approved by the Preparatory Committee and reported to the Ministry of Education for record.

Rules for Reviewing Proposals for the National Sports Conference

Article 1: These rules are based on Article 22 of the Rules of Procedure of the National Sports Conference.

Article 2: All proposals submitted for review shall be reviewed in groups according to their nature. The groups are tentatively set as follows:

(1) School Sports Group; (2) Public Sports Group; (3) Children's Sports Group; (4) Women's Sports Group; (5) National Martial Arts Group; (6) Sports Administration Group (7) Other

Article 3: The members of the Review Committee of each group shall be freely determined by the members, limited to two groups per person, and designated by the chairman when necessary.

Article 4: Each group shall have a chairman and a secretary, who shall be elected from among the members of each group.

Article 5: Each group may hold separate meetings for the convenience of review, and may also hold joint meetings with related groups.

Article 6: The meeting time of each group shall be determined by the chairman, but shall not conflict with the general assembly time.

Article 7: The meeting of each group shall be convened by the chairman.

Article 8: The secretary shall be responsible for organizing the reports and amendments of each group's review of the proposals.

Article 9: If members have opinions on various proposals, they may submit their opinions in writing to the chairman of the relevant review group for reference before the review.

Article 10: The review meeting must have more than half of the members of each group present to be convened.

Article 11: The resolution of the review meeting shall be passed with the consent of more than half of the members present. However, if each committee member has two or more opinions on the same proposal, if it is deemed necessary, the second most numerous opinion may be attached to the General Assembly.

Article 12: The review meeting may invite the original proposing member to attend the meeting to explain.

Article 13: For each case reviewed, the review meeting shall prepare a report on the review results and submit it to the Preparatory Committee for inclusion in the agenda. If amendments are deemed necessary, an amendment shall be drafted and printed for distribution to all members when it is submitted to the General Assembly.

Article 14: The review committee may recommend one representative for each review report or amendment to explain to the General Assembly.

Article 15: If any of the following circumstances occur in the review of the proposals by each group, the Review Committee shall submit it to the General Assembly for decision: (1) a proposal that is deemed unnecessary to be submitted; (2) a proposal that is deemed to be temporarily reserved.

Article 16: These rules shall be implemented after being approved by the Preparatory Committee and reported to the Ministry of Education for record.

Article 17: If there are any deficiencies or improprieties in these rules, they shall be amended by the Preparatory Committee or the General Assembly.

The Tenth World Olympic Games Inaugurated Today Due to Van's Defeat

Held in Los Angeles, USA, with Participants from Over Fifty Countries

Fifteen Types of Sports, China Sends Liu Changchun for the First Time

The long-awaited Tenth World Olympic Games were inaugurated in Los Angeles, California, USA, at 1:00 PM today. This time, participants include more than fifty countries of all sizes, with over two thousand athletes, fifteen types of sports, and more than one hundred and fifty events. Our country also sent athlete Liu Changchun and coach Song Junfu to participate. The National Sports Advancement Association also sent Secretary-General Shen Siliang to attend the opening ceremony. It is expected that the national emblems of various countries will flutter in the gentle breeze of the Pacific Ocean in the arena of world peace and war, to promote the great alliance of world nations.

Coubertin's Statement on the Restoration of the World Olympic Games French Baron Coubertin, who restored the World Olympic Games, made the following statement regarding this Games:

The true essence of the struggle for survival lies not in temporary victory, but in eternal struggle, and it is especially important that it be carried out in a proper manner. If this principle is passed on, humanity will be able to incorporate health, and the world will be able to achieve a city of well-being. The Olympic Games are to show the world the true meaning of survival, and also to use this true meaning to guide and achieve the great purpose of the Olympics. I hope that the spirit of harmony and sympathy can be fully expressed, so that the light of the Olympics can shine on the future, the friendship between nations can grow with each year, and the gospel of humanity can become more and more sincere and pure.

The Gate of the Olympic Arena

Prizes The prizes for the World Olympic Games are divided into medals and certificates. The top three in each individual and team sport receive awards: (A) Individual Competition, (1) First Place: Gold Medal and Certificate, (2) Second Place: Silver Medal and Certificate, (3) Third Place: Bronze Medal and Certificate. (B) Team Competition, (1) First Place: Team Certificate, Team Members Receive Gold Medals and Certificates, (2) Second Place: Team Certificate, Team Members Receive Silver Medals and Certificates, (3) Third Place: Team Certificate, Team Members Receive Bronze Medals and Certificates. Team members can only receive awards if they participated in the competition. The names of the athletes are engraved on the venue of the Games. All participating athletes and staff receive a commemorative medal. Athletes with special skills or who create new records in the preliminary rounds but do not win awards will be recommended by the International Committee to the Organizing Committee to issue special certificates to show encouragement.

Trophy The World Olympic Games does not have a system of total trophies. The names of the top six winners in each sport are inscribed on the certificate of honor in alphabetical order. The certificate is kept by the International Olympic Committee. When people say that a certain country won the World Olympic Games trophy, it refers to the track and field trophy, because track and field is the main part of the Games.

The Olympic Flag The Olympic flag has a white background with red, yellow, blue, white, and black circles embroidered on it, interlocked with each other to represent the great gathering of the five races of the five continents of the world, and to promote the feeling of mutual friendship. This flag was donated by Belgium in 1920. From the opening day of the Games, it is hung together with the national flags of all participating countries around the sports arena. A flagpole is erected in the arena, dedicated to raising the Olympic flag. This flag is usually kept by the city hall of the host country's meeting place. It is taken out and handed over to the host country of the next Games at the next Games.

Mark of Victory When the final of each sport ends, the national flag of the winning country must be raised, and at the same time the military band will play the national anthem of the winning country. All athletes and spectators in the arena must pay the highest respect in the same arena.

Tennis and Football The World Olympic Games does not have tennis competitions because there is an international tennis tournament, the Davis Cup, and an international individual tennis tournament, Wimbledon, every year. As for football, it was originally included, and the football competition of the Ninth World Games was particularly prosperous, so our country initially planned to send a football team to participate, but it was decided to cancel it due to rule issues. If the World Football Association is willing to slightly modify the rules to meet the needs of amateur sports, it can also be included. However, when the World Football Association met in Budapest, Hungary, the meeting decided not to change its attitude, so this Games ultimately failed to be included.

Next Games to be Held in Germany Los Angeles, 28th - The Olympic Committee met here today and decided that the next Games (1936) will be held in Germany. The location of the Twelfth Games in 1940 has not yet been decided. Japan and twelve countries have proposed holding the Games in their own country.

Nurmi Prohibited from Participating (Los Angeles, 28th) Finnish long-distance runner Nurmi has had problems with his eligibility as an amateur athlete due to receiving financial instruction. The International Amateur Athletic Federation reviewed the matter today and did not recognize Nurmi as an amateur athlete, and officially announced that he was prohibited from attending. Nurmi holds the world record for 5,000 meters at 14 minutes and 28.2 seconds, and 10,000 meters at 30 minutes and 6.2 seconds. He was planning to participate in the marathon at this Olympics, but was not allowed to attend, which is a pity for running fans. (Editor's Note) Nurmi has participated in the World Games four times, but has never participated in the marathon. Nurmi had previously declared that he would participate in the marathon at this year's Tenth Games to end his lifelong athletic career. This kind of behavior is very popular. Now, unexpectedly, he is not allowed to participate because of violating amateur rules, which is the biggest regret in Nurmi's athletic career.

Gold Prices Fluctuate

The Final Session Increased by Slightly More Than Two Taels Yesterday, gold prices tended to rise again, but the market conditions were unpredictable and erratic, hovering around 750 taels all day, with a difference of only two or three taels. The final tally showed an increase of two taels, but industry sentiment remained hesitant. In the morning, although silver bars rose, and American silver did not change, it was actually due to frequent drops in exchange rates, so it opened high. After that, the ups and downs varied slightly by one or two taels. As for bills of exchange, British and American currencies were stable, with banks alternately buying and selling, making the market even more scattered, and prices fluctuating around 51 taels, as if the bulls and bears were evenly matched. Almost all of the August contracts that had not been cleared were settled, due to the bulls adding five cents. The daily situation is recorded below.

The Morning Opened with an Increase of Three Taels and One Cent Starting from 751 taels and three cents for September, an increase of three taels and one cent, because American silver was as before, but large bars returned by one-sixteenth to one-eighth, without being affected. Especially since British and American exchange rates repeatedly plummeted by more than two and seventy-five hundredths, and because Zhifeng, Yonghong, Kangyong, and others bought in, it increased to 51 taels and eight cents. However, there were also quite a few sell orders, and the price fell slightly by one tael to 50 taels and six cents. Because Hengyu, Zhifeng, Yongtongchun, Yifengyong, and goods companies rushed to buy, and American silver companies bought 4375 worth of British gold for October, and the industry also bought 6875 worth of American gold for August, and China Bank absorbed 4375 worth of British gold for November, the price rose to 52 taels and three cents. Unexpectedly, HSBC and others released 875 worth of American gold for September, and Daxing, Yongyuanheng, and Hengxing took the opportunity to sell, causing it to fall back to 50 taels. At 9:30, HSBC quoted British gold higher by one and two-fifths of a penny, and American gold unchanged, to offset the small exchange rate difference. At this time, Tongchun bought in again at 50 taels and seven cents. Afterwards, the situation was chaotic, fluctuating around 50 taels, with different numbers of purchases and sales by each firm, but there were no large batches. It is estimated that Hengxing, Fuxing, Yongdaxingyong, and Zhifengyong successively sold, and because 6875 worth of American gold for this month could be settled, and British gold for October even required half a penny, the price fell by two taels, and at 10:10 it was 48 taels and six cents. After this, there seemed to be an upward trend, but people's hearts were uncertain and buying and selling were still very different. However, the price broke through the 50 tael mark because the bank absorbed 1875 worth of American gold for November, and HSBC absorbed half a penny of British gold, until after 11:30, Yuanxingyong, Hengyu, Yuanmaoyong, Futaiheng, and Yuantai all purchased. At noon, it was 50 taels and seven cents, and then closed at 50 taels and six cents. In the afternoon, speculation was weak. The market opened at 50 taels and four cents, with Hengyu and Yuanxingyong buying, and rising to 51 taels and three cents. Huabi absorbed 75 worth of American gold for August, and Wheat absorbed 0625 for October. Then, due to the goods companies selling to cover their positions, it lost one tael to 50 taels. After 3:00, Bombay bought 18 and a half worth of British gold for October, and Hengyu and others bought in, adding one tael. At 3:30, it was 51 taels and one cent. Ultimately, due to the activity of sellers, and American gold seemed to be loosening, the brokers bought 75 to 8125 for August. Zhifengyong and Tongchun both sold. As the market approached closing, it was 50 taels and two cents. At 4:00, the closing price was 50 taels and five cents, higher than the previous evening by two taels and three cents, then suppressed to 50 taels. The maximum for the day was 52 taels and three cents, and the minimum was 48 taels and six cents, a difference of three taels and seven cents. The red bar increased by nine taels.

The Official Price Was Suppressed by Sixty-Seven Taels The official price was still 817 taels, suppressed by 66-67 taels, and 67 taels in the afternoon, two taels less than the previous day. Registered prices were 54 taels to 50 taels. Water replenishment was calculated at 50 taels for the whole day.

Buyers Seemed to Occupy the Majority In on-the-table transactions, buyers seemed to be more numerous. Yuanxingyong, Yuanmaoyong, Hengyu, Yuantai, Futaiheng, Zhaofengchang, Hongkangyong, Tongchun, Hengxingyuan, Tongtaichang, and Yifengyong all bought in. The rest were mixed, but there were no large transactions. On that day, the Dalian gang only had two or three hundred bars. The Cantonese gang, like Hengxing, sold more than three hundred bars, and there were few buyers. A speculator named Wu sold slightly in the morning market, but bought to cover positions.

Gold Firms First Bought, Then Sold

Yesterday, silver prices rose in British currency and were stable in American currency, and exchange rates had plummeted for three consecutive days (a total of more than four and eighty-seven hundredths), so the trend of British currency loosening and American currency stabilizing in this port emerged. HSBC quoted British gold higher by half a notch (one and two-fifths of a penny) at one shilling and eight and one-fifth of a penny, Indian exchange added half a yuan, German exchange decreased slightly by six and one-fourth, Japanese exchange decreased by two and a half, Singaporean exchange fell by one tael, Hong Kong exchange did not change, and American gold remained at 29 yuan and three-seventy-fifth. General Situation of Cotton Crops in Tianjin

In Tianjin, the rainfall in the spring was insufficient, and the sowing was later. After sowing, some were damaged by hail. Generally speaking, it is still smooth, and all places can expect a normal harvest. The cotton fields in the (Xihe) area have decreased by 10% compared to last year. Insufficient rainfall caused poor development after sowing, so American cotton was replanted. The cotton fields in that area have decreased by about 20%. The development in the Daqing River basin is very good. In the (Yuhe) area, the planting area of coarse velvet cotton is the same as in normal years, while American cotton has decreased by 10%. The climate was favorable after sowing, and the development was good. In the (Shanji) area, the cotton fields have increased by 15% compared to last year. The weather was dry during planting, but it was smooth afterwards, and the cotton trees developed well. The harvest is expected to be no different from last year.

A Glimpse of the July Yarn Settlement

And a Retrospective of the Entire Process

The July yarn futures contract began trading on May 2nd, with prices around 154.5 taels. It rose by over 6 taels initially, but then due to the bankruptcy of rural areas in China, economic decline, and new lows in American cotton prices, raw cotton prices plummeted, causing a lack of confidence. Actual sales stagnated, and coupled with aggressive and cheap Japanese yarn sales, some yarn factories sold off several thousand bales. The market became increasingly weak, with prices dropping directly from 55 taels to 38.3 taels. At this point, people's anxiety reached its peak, and many expected to see exceptionally low prices. Midway through, American cotton prices rebounded, and demand from southern ports greatly increased. Yunnan merchants, benefiting from abundant agricultural harvests, heavily purchased 10-count coarse yarn. Merchants from Guangdong and Yunnan rushed to buy, searching without end, and factories were overwhelmed. The remaining spot goods were almost completely swept away. At the same time, Hunan also showed signs of improvement. Buyers, seeing the shortage of spot yarn, shifted to purchasing August, September, and October futures, and sentiment reached a boiling point. Rongxing and Changfeng, two major yarn firms, heavily went long, absorbing an estimated 30,000 to 40,000 bales, and prices rose from over 38 taels to 54.2 taels (the highest). The price range during these two months was as high as 15.9 taels, which can be considered significant. This situation was entirely driven by actual demand. The settlement price was over 153 taels, with a remaining quantity of only 3,700 bales. Among these, 2,950 bales were self-settled, 750 bales were delivered by Gengfeng, and 450 bales were received by Rongxing. The brokers and quantities for both buyers and sellers are listed below:

Cotton: The July cotton futures contract started trading in early May at a price between 31.8 and 31.9 taels, rising by over 3 taels. Shortly after, due to stagnation in actual demand and a drop in yarn prices, factories had no need to purchase. Furthermore, the American Cotton Bureau announced that it would sell off half of its 1.3 million bales of American cotton. Coupled with favorable weather conditions for new cotton, progress was smooth, and prices fell from over 6 cents to 5 cents. In July, prices broke through the 5-cent mark, setting a new record unseen in a century. People around the world showed great panic. As a result, cotton futures experienced sharp selling pressure, and longs were unable to sustain their positions, leading to a gradual and rapid decline in prices. Moreover, the China Cotton Corporation, having purchased spot cotton in various producing areas, and seeing that factories had no intention to buy, had no choice but to sell futures contracts to manage risk. Recently, the market has continued to decline, and the Ningbo Yao Hua Exchange has also been affected by global trends. There was a lack of buyers, with only sellers present. With both sides deadlocked, it was difficult for the market to open. The exchange authorities tried to maintain the market by purchasing cotton and selling futures in Shanghai, further weakening the cotton futures market. The lowest price reached 27 taels. Subsequently, gold prices rebounded, and American cotton, due to excessive rainfall and severe insect infestations, rebounded from 5 cents to 6.2 cents, showing a sharp recovery. The highest price reached 31.95 taels, and large accounts bought to go long. The settlement price at the end of the month was over 31 taels, with a remaining quantity of only 18,700 dan. Among these, 15,000 to 16,000 dan were settled by fellow traders, and actual deliveries were only a little over 1,000 dan. The goods consisted of Shandong cotton, Zhengzhou cotton, and Shaanxi cotton. Yong'an Factory received the most, and China Cotton Trading Company delivered the most. Other deliveries were minimal. Flour Market Rallies Sharply After the Second Session

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market, prices for all months initially showed stability before rising. Prices for foreign wheat quoted in Chicago were good, up 2 to 3 jiao, and Canadian wheat was up about 4 fen. In addition, buyers initially remained inactive, and there were no surprises in opening prices. However, after the second session, due to purchases from Tianjin cigarette and other merchants for both near-term and far-term deliveries, sentiment rebounded, and prices rose steadily. Many speculators also took advantage of this opportunity to aggressively buy in each session, so the price increase was quite sharp. Observing the later situation, it is said that foreign wheat markets are estimated to decline, so whether or not they will come to China later is a matter of great concern. As a result, the current month rose by 2 fen and 2.5 li compared to the previous day, August rose by 1 fen and 7 li, September rose by 2 fen, October rose by 1 fen and 2.5 li, November rose by 1 fen and 5 li, and December rose by 1 fen and 2.5 li.

Some Longs Return 期 Wheat

Yesterday, after the opening of the wheat futures market, although foreign wheat rose by 2 to 3 jiao and Canadian wheat rose by 4 fen, general sentiment was that wheat had risen sharply the previous day, while flour prices had not risen by much, so some longs gradually sold off, causing the market to slightly weaken. However, inland customers showed greater stability in their thinking. It is difficult to expect a strong surge in selling. If foreign wheat is not cost-effective, then the standard market value cannot be considered high, so returning to a good path is not surprising. As a result, August was down 1 fen compared to the previous day, September was down 3 fen, October was down 2 fen, and November and December were down 2 fen. The spot wheat market has become chaotic due to differences in quality and origin. Opening prices vary greatly. For example, Guzhen high-quality wheat, due to its scarcity, opened at 3 taels and 4 qian, which is similar to the standard price. The remaining Zhenjiang wheat opened at 3 taels, 1 qian, and 7 fen, Shuangfeng wheat opened at 3 taels, 1 qian, and 5 fen, Taicang wheat opened at 3 taels and 5 fen, and Pudong wheat opened at 2 taels and 8 qian and 8 fen.
