Various Parties Prepare to Establish Epidemic Hospitals

Wu Xingya and Others Prepare to Establish an Epidemic Hospital. Wu Xingya, Director of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, in view of the rampant epidemics after the war, and the recent hot weather, which is becoming more fierce, the epidemic-stricken civilians are in urgent need of relief. Therefore, in his private capacity, he united with Shanghai celebrities to initiate the organization of an epidemic hospital. He has been running around for the past few days and has some clues. Yesterday, he specially invited the initiators to the Xinghualou on Fourth Horse Road to discuss fundraising methods. Yu Qiaqing, Du Yuesheng, Yang Xiaotian, Chen Renhe, Qin Runqing, Wang Binyan, Gu Xinyi, Zhu Yaxiong, Zhang Binghui, and more than ten other people were present. Other initiators, Wang Xiaolai, Zhang Xiaolin, Lin Kanghou, Wang Yiting, Pan Gongzhan, Wang Yansong, Chen Bingqian, etc., were unable to attend due to leaving Shanghai for business. The discussion was very successful. It is said that Mr. Du Yuesheng, in order to speed up the process, is willing to advance 5,000 yuan to start the business first. The remaining initiators will raise funds separately. It is said that Mr. Zhang Binghui will temporarily manage the hospital affairs, and Mr. Zhu Yaxiong, a famous doctor in Shanghai, will be in charge of medical affairs. Mr. Zhu is not only well-versed in medicine, but also enthusiastic about social welfare. The doctors hired by the hospital are all famous doctors in Shanghai. They will survey the location in Zhabei within days and actively carry out the work. They should be able to start treatment at the beginning of next month.

Overseas Chinese Federation Establishes Epidemic Hospital. The pain suffered by the citizens of Shanghai during the January 28 Incident is indescribable. Although normalcy is gradually recovering, the prevalence of cholera, which causes rapid death, makes citizens uneasy. The Shanghai Overseas Chinese Federation, in view of this, decided at a meeting yesterday to establish an epidemic hospital in order to facilitate the citizens. It plans to select a suitable location in Zhabei and invite well-known Chinese doctors who have returned from overseas to provide medical treatment and free medicine. It is now actively underway and is said to be opening soon.

Nanhui Epidemic Hospital of the Red Cross Society Established. After the Japanese invasion, the poison was extremely deep. All parts of Songhu are plagued by epidemics, and Nanhui, which is close to Songhu, is also affected by the remnants of the poison. Recently, epidemics have been seen everywhere, and deaths have followed one another. Xu Baiyi, the president of the Red Cross branch in the county, works in a certain department of the National Government, and specially donated a large sum of money to prepare for the establishment of the Red Cross Epidemic Hospital. Last month, he had exhausted all efforts to prepare, so he came to the Shanghai General Association to consult with doctors. Dr. Zhou Hongzhang introduced Zhang Dichen and Zhou Honggeng, high-achieving students of Southeast Medical College, as the directors of medical affairs of the hospital. They went to work a few days ago. The hospital is purely charitable and does not charge any fees.

Cholera Kills People

The Lai Family Dies Seven People

The weather has been hot recently, and epidemics are prevalent. Therefore, it is not uncommon for people who are infected to die in an instant. There is a gem merchant named Lai in the Jiumu Di area of the city. His family of eleven, including two servants, died a total of seven people within ten days. The details are excerpted below:

Lai, a gem merchant from Nanjing, is about fifty years old, and his wife is of the same age. He has seven children, the oldest being twenty-one years old and the youngest being ten years old. The other children are all one or two years apart. The family has two servants and lives alone in a house. He has a gem shop in Qingdao and buys and sells gems in Shanghai, which is quite prosperous. Therefore, he has accumulated 40,000 to 50,000 yuan and can be called a happy family.

Wife Falls Ill First. A week ago, his wife suddenly contracted cholera. Although he sought medical treatment, the epidemic was very severe. She died within a few hours. While the funeral was being arranged, the wife had not yet been coffined. A son contracted the same disease. Lai was extremely anxious and hired Chinese and Western doctors to treat him, but it was still ineffective. He died within two days. Within ten days, one wife and five sons died one after another.

Servant Sent to the Hospital. Suddenly, the servant contracted cholera the day before yesterday. Neighbors and friends advised Lai to send the servant to the hospital for treatment. Unexpectedly, after the servant was sent to the hospital, Lai himself fell ill and was bedridden. Although several famous doctors in Shanghai were hired every day, the doctors were helpless. Seeing this disease, relatives and friends were afraid and did not dare to visit. After being repeatedly advised by a close friend, he went to a certain hospital for treatment yesterday. Seven people died. Only two sons and one servant were left in the family. One of the sons also contracted cholera a few hours after his father went to the hospital for treatment. When he fell ill, they all said that they had headaches and fever. The patients had the same symptoms. This son also died within a few hours, and no one was left to take care of the funeral. Later, relatives and friends helped to take care of it. Within ten days, a family of eleven died one wife and six sons. He himself is still in a dangerous situation and it is not known if he can escape the danger.

Commercial Corps Overseas Chinese Cup Competition News

Chen Shixia of Shanghai scored 88 points, ranking first. The Overseas Chinese Cup was donated by Mr. Ge Leilie, the former captain of the Chinese team of the International Commercial Corps, so it is also known as the Ge Leilie Cup. It is specially for the Chinese commercial corps in various ports in the Far East to compete in shooting skills. An inter-port remote competition is held once a year to determine who owns the cup. Over the years, Shanghai and Singapore have competed fiercely, and the Shanghai Chinese team has always been known for its superior shooting skills. Therefore, Shanghai has won against Singapore for six consecutive years. It is said that in this year's competition, Shanghai shot at the Hongkou shooting range yesterday morning. Corps consultant Hu Yunqiu, staff officer Henk Leif, adjutant Marston Ross, and the executive committee of the International Rifle Association, Karasso, personally attended to supervise the venue and record scores to show their solemnity. The result was a total of 808 points, which is a particularly good result compared to 795 points last year. There is no doubt that Shanghai will retain the championship in this year's competition. The names and scores of the Shanghai players in this competition are recorded below: Lieutenant Chen Shixia scored 88 points, Lieutenant Li Yushu scored 84 points, Sergeant Gu Wenzhong scored 83 points, trainee He Bingcheng scored 81 points, Sergeant Zhang Naibin scored 81 points, team member Xu Baozong scored 80 points, Sergeant Zhou Changshan scored 80 points, Sergeant Wang Chungang scored 79 points, Sergeant Lu Zhenting scored 77 points, Sergeant Xu Shaomei scored 75 points. Looking at the scores, Lieutenant Chen Shixia was the best. Mr. Chen is the new captain of the team. He has been working in the Corps for many years and has not been shooting for a long time. This small test is as good as his skills back then, which is commendable and truly outstanding.

Husband Shoots Adulterer Case

The Adulterer is Severely Injured and Unable to Appear in Court

The Hearing is Postponed to August 8th

Wang Xingsheng, a local carpenter residing at No. 2 Wangjiazhai, Gaolangqiao, because his wife, Wan, was being seduced by Yao Guishan, a rattan craftsman from No. 52 next door, and abducted in March of this year to Zhoupu, Pudong, was found and brought back by Wang. On the afternoon of the 3rd of this month, at 2 p.m., she was again lured to a clandestine meeting at the 16th Piling, which Wang discovered. Concealing a pistol, he followed her to No. 33 Yuxing Street, outside the Xiaodongmen in the French Concession. When he saw Yao, Wang immediately drew his pistol and fired two shots into Yao's lower back. He then turned around and tried to escape in a rickshaw, but was intercepted by the police near Xinkaihe, who arrested Wang and his wife and took them to the police station. Yao was sent to Renji Hospital for treatment. The next day, the police sent Wang and his wife to the Second Special District Court for interrogation and detention, pending the victim's recovery. The situation has been reported in the previous newspaper. Yesterday, Judge Wang Gangxu presided over a continued trial in the Criminal Division. He first asked the police detectives about the victim's injuries. It was reported that the victim, Yao Guishan, had not yet recovered from his injuries. The doctor said that due to his weak physical condition, he could not undergo surgery to remove the bullets and needed to rest before a decision could be made. Then, Wang Xingsheng's mother-in-law, Wan Zhou, was called as a witness. She testified that "Xingsheng is my son-in-law, and Wan is my daughter. They have been married for nine years and have two children, a nine-year-old boy and a dead baby girl. My daughter had an affair with Yao Guishan, which I knew nothing about. Yao never came to my house. I don't know anything about Xingsheng shooting Yao Guishan with a pistol. The pistol was not taken from my house; I don't know where it came from. My daughter was found and brought back from Zhoupu in March and worked at the Dasheng Factory, living in my house. I don't know if Xingsheng came to my house on the day of the incident. I was working in the field and don't know if he and my wife discussed shooting Yao Guishan. I know nothing about it." Wang Wan was ordered to appear in court. She testified that on that day, Yao Guishan came to Linqing Road to ask me to go to the 16th Piling. My husband did not go with me and did not come to my mother's house. The pistol was held by my husband. This gun was actually given to me by Yao this spring, instructing me to kill my husband. I couldn't bear to do it, so I put it in the house. My husband didn't know that I went to the 16th Piling that day. I probably came to look for me. I didn't discuss it with my husband beforehand. Wang Xingsheng testified that the pistol was taken from the bed in the house. At about 1 p.m. that day, I went to my mother-in-law's house and didn't see my wife. Someone said she went south, so I went home, took the pistol, and chased her to Yuxing Street in the 16th Piling and shot Yao. I didn't discuss it with my wife beforehand. Now it is wrong for me to hit him, but he was the first to be bad. I beg the court to forgive me, etc." Finally, the defendants' lawyers, Zhang Ji and others, stated that "if the victim dies as a result of the injury, the defendant should bear criminal responsibility. However, the hospital is not providing medical treatment now, and if the death is delayed as a result, that is another matter, and the court should pay attention to it." Judge Wang verified the statements and ordered the hearing to be postponed to August 8th. The defendants were remanded in custody.

Opening of Shenjiahang Stores

The conflict between the Shenjiahang shop guards and the militia, which led to a market strike, has been going on for several days. Yesterday morning at 9:00 a.m., Yu Yuanjue, a staff member of the Municipal Government Reorganization Committee, and Yao Benyuan, the director of the Seventh District Second Precinct, persuaded the stores to reopen, and they all resumed business as usual. The cause of the strike will now be traced and stated below to clarify the truth. It was discovered that after 10 p.m. on the 24th, someone was singing obscene songs on the street in front of the Chi Peide Pharmacy of Shenjiahang. The police officer on duty, No. 4769, of the Seventh District Second Precinct, believed that singing obscene songs was harmful to public morals and violated police regulations, so he stepped forward to dissuade the singing and the audience, who immediately dispersed. However, Lu Shengxian, a partner in the Chi Peide Pharmacy opened by Wang Shishan, the platoon leader of the town's militia, suddenly had a conflict with the police officers. Afterwards, the patrol officer reprimanded the police officer, saying that his actions at the time were inappropriate. After the station chief returned to the station, he learned about the previous situation and punished the police officer with twenty slaps as a warning. He also invited Wang Shishan, the owner of the Chi Peide Pharmacy, to the station to explain what happened. When Wang returned, he encountered the reprimanded police officer, and the two sides disagreed, resulting in another conflict. Ji Longsheng, a police officer from the same shift, saw his brother being bullied and stepped forward to help. Afterwards, the precinct believed that the police officers' actions were crude and did not meet the standards of a police officer, so it sent the two police officers who caused the trouble to the Public Security Bureau for punishment.

Introduction to the Publication of New Books on National Goods

The China National Goods Guidance Institute, affiliated with the China Vocational Education Society, has been established for more than half a year and has spared no effort in promoting, introducing, investigating, and guiding national goods. In addition to displaying products from various national goods factories in specially made display cases at the institute for public viewing, it has recently taken a further step to provide a faithful introduction to make it easier for people in distant lands to understand and purchase. It has compiled and printed 30,000 copies of the "General Catalog of Shanghai National Goods Manufactured Products," which list the addresses, product types, telephone and telegraph numbers, and trademark styles of various well-known national goods factories in the city. It is divided into categories such as dyeing and weaving, daily necessities, food and beverages, books and newspapers, printing, Western medicine and cosmetics, machinery, and construction, and includes advertisements from each factory for easier verification. It has now been published and bound in two thick volumes. To facilitate widespread circulation, copies will be given away free of charge upon request. For mail orders, please attach a 3-cent postage stamp and send it to the China National Goods Guidance Institute, No. 80 Hualong Road, Shanghai, and it will be mailed to you immediately. Comrades who love and use national goods should have one copy per person.

Direct Access by Shanghai-Minhang Bus

Submission

Preface to the Siku Grand Dictionary by Wang Yunwu

Because Wen Tianxiang said, "Where to start with the Seventeen Histories?" Therefore, modern people often say, "Where to start reading the Twenty-Four Histories?" In fact, the Twenty-Four Histories only have more than 3,200 volumes and more than 28 million words, which is not much compared to the more than 79,000 volumes and more than 700 million words of the Siku Quanshu. Even the Siku Quanshu, if typeset, printed, and bound in ordinary fonts and formats, would amount to at most 10,000 volumes, which is even less compared to the libraries in Paris, London, Washington, etc., which have more than 4 million books. But we have never heard readers in those libraries—especially readers in the Washington Library of Congress—say "Where to start reading?" Last year, when I traveled to Europe and the United States, I spent ten days reading books in the Washington Library. I actually browsed through more than 1,000 books and magazines on scientific management in the library's collection of more than 4 million books. Some people suspect that this may not be true. In fact, it is not at all false, because the library's catalog cards are compiled very completely. As long as you review the various catalog cards in the catalog room according to direct and indirect related titles, you will see all kinds of important books, collections, essays, and related categories, as well as the names, volumes, versions, publication dates, content, nature, abstracts, and related works of each book, as well as the names, eras, qualifications, academic achievements, and other works of each author. After reading the various catalog cards of each book, we already understand its general idea, and then we take them separately and borrow the books that must be read. Then, we check the index of each book to find the parts that must be read. Thus, the books that must be read account for only one ten-thousandth of the entire collection, and the parts that must be read account for only one thousandth or one hundredth of the books that must be read. In this way, searching for one grain of rice in the vast ocean of books is not difficult, and there will be no difficulty in "Where to start reading?"

In addition to these convenient reference library catalog cards, there are many other reading tools in Europe and the United States, such as book dictionaries, essay indexes, and book and newspaper abstracts. Most of their compilations are arranged alphabetically, which is convenient for checking and can be understood at a glance. Therefore, the reading community will not have the difficulty of "Where to start reading?" Chinese bibliography has always been known for its sophistication, and there are many works on bibliography, but they often detail one book and one thing, making it difficult for readers to get a general idea. Moreover, the classification is too broad, making checking very inconvenient. There is no book dictionary arranged alphabetically that can give people a general idea. Liang Rengong (Liang Qichao) had a plan to compile a Grand Dictionary of Chinese Books before his death, but he did not complete it. Mr. Yang Jialuo is well-versed in bibliography and is also engaged in the compilation of the Grand Dictionary of Chinese Books, making continuous progress. He first completed a Siku Grand Dictionary, using the general catalog of the Siku Quanshu in 200 volumes as the record, and the books and authors recorded in the Cunmu as the scope. Each book name and person name within the scope is established as a separate entry, with more than 17,000 entries and more than 2.5 million words. The book name entry includes the number of volumes, appendices and their number of volumes, the name of the author or annotator, category, annotation, and version. The author entry includes the names of the books written or annotated, the author's era, origin, a short biography, the names of works not included in the Siku, and reference books for the author's detailed biography. In addition, in order to facilitate checking, it is arranged according to the dictionary style, using my Four-Corner Numeral Indexing Method. After the draft is completed and sent to print, I am asked to write a preface. I believe that this book is consistent with the dictionary-style book dictionaries of Europe and the United States mentioned above. It is the first most applicable and most convenient book dictionary in China. It can eliminate the difficulty of "Where to start reading?" that the Chinese reading community has always felt. Therefore, on the one hand, I hope that Mr. Yang will complete the work of the Grand Dictionary of Chinese Books as soon as possible. On the other hand, I am very happy to introduce this book to the reading community.

This book was previously sold by subscription. The academic community, such as Academia Sinica (President Cai Yuanpei said it was an extremely useful work), the Ministry of Education, Central University, Peking University (President Jiang Menglin said that Chinese academic thought is embodied in it), Tsinghua University, Yanjing University, Sun Yat-sen University, Zhejiang University, Wuhan University, the Palace Museum, Peking Library, Oriental Library, Nanjing Library, and provincial, municipal, county, and private libraries, have all subscribed to it. Its value and necessity can be seen here. The upper volume has already been published, and the lower volume will be printed soon. It is published by the Chinese Book Grand Dictionary Editorial Office, No. 17 Yongji Lane, Avenue Road, Shanghai, and sold by Shanghai Kaiming Bookstore and its branches in various places. The price is 24 yuan, and the subscription price is 18 yuan.

Letter

To the editor, we saw in your newspaper's local news column, "Yesterday the price of Chinese yarn in the Yarn and Cloth Exchange rose sharply, while the price of Japanese yarn suddenly fell." According to our exchange's market, the regular buying and selling is based on yarns such as the Ren Zhong brand listed in the grade table. The statement that the price of Japanese yarn suddenly fell should not refer to the transactions of brokers in our exchange's market, and there may be a misunderstanding. This letter is for your information, and we hope that you will publish it in the letter column for correction. Sincerely, Shanghai Chinese Yarn and Cloth Exchange, July 29th.

Free Talk

Two or three Branches of Chat

Common Sayings and Their Origins

— Zhan Lu

With nothing to do during the long summer, studying common sayings from various places is also a way to pass the time. Common sayings can be general or specific; general common sayings are not limited to a particular place, while specific common sayings are only used in a certain area. People from other places will not understand them, simply because the common sayings contain a backstory.

"Xiao Er of the Qi Ziqing Family Never Says Good Things" || This is a Suzhou common saying, the origin of which is found in the "Double Gold Ingots" storytelling song. The Suzhou lawyer Qi Ziqing hired a servant boy named Xiao Er, who never said good things. Since then, whenever people encounter someone who doesn't say good things, Suzhou people would mock them as "Xiao Er of the Qi Ziqing Family".

"The All-Heaven God of Huangjin Dam is Fake to the Core" || This is a Yangzhou common saying, recorded in the "False All-Heaven God" novel written by Shi Tianji. It is said that in Huangjin Dam, Yangzhou, a country bumpkin claimed to be the descent of the All-Heaven God, stirring up the people who all went to burn incense. Before long, Governor Jin saw through the deception and exposed the fraud, and the affair ended in failure. Later, whenever people encounter something fraudulent, they say, "The All-Heaven God of Huangjin Dam is fake to the core".

"The Dragon Causes Disaster, the Mangy Turtle Takes the Blame" This is a Jinling common saying, found in the "Supplement to the Firm Gourd Collection" by Chu Shinong. It is said that in the early Ming Dynasty, the Dragon caused trouble around Shangqing River. Because Emperor Zhu was very superstitious, the Ministry of Public Works dared not say dragon in their report, only saying that large turtles were the problem. The Emperor, because the character for turtle was the same as the Yuan Dynasty's Yuan, ordered fishermen to kill all the turtles. Fishermen fished for turtles, using bottomless jars to cover the turtles' heads, rendering them immobile. Later, whenever encountering a situation where one thing is substituted for another, people say: "The dragon causes disaster, the mangy turtle takes the blame."

"The Shiitake Mushroom Mountain Cat Cries Blindly" | This is a Wenzhou common saying, found in "Miscellaneous Poems from Two Windows" by Wang Chaoqing. It is said that in the mountains of Ou and Yue, shiitake mushrooms are widely cultivated; to prevent rat damage, people always capture wildcats, gouge out their eyes, and raise them in the mountains. Once the cats are blinded, they do not go elsewhere, only crying blindly day and night. The rats, hearing the sound, avoid the area. Later, whenever people encounter ignorant people shouting nonsense without end, they say: "The shiitake mushroom mountain cat cries blindly."

Slogans on the Soil in the Trenches

— Wang Yu

During the January 28th Incident, our 19th Route Army bravely resisted, holding out with isolated troops against the enemy's several times larger forces for as long as thirty-two days and nights. This greatly surprised the enemy, and even European and American military experts were amazed. Enemy newspapers especially praised the trenches dug by our army, calling them "of a certain country's style". Soldiers lying in the trenches were not threatened by artillery fire, causing the enemy to waste ammunition. Airplanes also could not see the trenches, so their bombs missed their targets. The soldiers lying in the trenches could wait at ease for the enemy to approach, then leap out and win as easily as reaching into a pocket to take something. Our army's ability to win with fewer men was truly not accidental. A friend of mine went to the front lines during the war and entered the trenches himself. According to him, the trenches were very spacious, and the soldiers inside were exceptionally calm, not paying attention to the enemy's frequent bombardment. They would not fight unless the enemy launched an attack. Therefore, foreign newspapers commented that the January 28th Incident was a "fake war", even "humorous", because the continuous sound of gunfire in the war zone came from the enemy, while our army rarely retaliated. It was as if a strong man was using his fists and feet against a weak man, but the weak man did not use the same violence against the strong man, yet still managed to win. Therefore, the soldiers in the trenches were even leisurely, some using porcelain shards from broken bowls to embed words into the soil as slogans, such as "Defend Our Land", "Drive the Japanese Imperialist Army Out of Our Territory", "Respond Calmly", "Vow to Live and Die with This Trench", and "Wash Away the Shame of Non-Resistance", showing great ingenuity. How could one not win when facing such a formidable enemy with such calmness? If Shirakawa had not ambushed Liuhe and had engaged in a frontal assault, our army, though small, would not have retreated. Moreover, if the government had sent reinforcements earlier and heavily defended Liuhe, even if Shirakawa had attacked with heavy forces, wanting to attack our army's rear, Liuhe would have been heavily defended, and we would not have retreated. But alas, the government did not send reinforcements, letting the miraculous feat of thirty-two days and nights of bloody battle be ruined in one fell swoop. Is this not greatly regrettable?

The Second Flood

— Huang Ren

The recent floods in England have prompted research by scientists. According to one expert, there will be a second flood within 30,000 or 40,000 years, turning the entire world into a swamp. Saltwater will sweep across the five continents, with only a few pieces of dry land remaining on the highlands. The Netherlands will be completely submerged. The Buckingham Palace and Westminster Abbey in England will become aquariums, with fish swimming back and forth because most of the British Isles will be under water. The Sahara Desert, which is extremely arid, will also turn into an ocean. Only the tips of New York's skyscrapers will be visible above the water.

According to some scientists, the previous Ice Age has only passed halfway. The climate of the world is already turning warmer. The large ice floes in the Arctic and Antarctic Oceans are gradually melting and drifting into other oceans. The ice floes in the Arctic and Antarctic originally covered 12 million square miles, but half of that has already melted. If the other half completely melts, the world will inevitably undergo a transformation. Even now, many coastal villages in England have been submerged in the water over the past twenty-five years. In one place, you can still see the spire of a church.

Cold Talk in Hot Weather

— Yang Yusheng

The map of the Northeast Provinces has changed. It's gradually slipping out of the blurred minds of the Chinese people. No wonder a large number of Japanese goods are flooding into the ports along the Yangtze River. Since the world already has such a useless group who don't strive for self-improvement, why would Japan love China and not show off its might in Rehe? Some say Rehe is already in critical condition, while others say Rehe should be safe. Especially Nanjing, which still maintains a nonchalant attitude, only exhausting Liu Adou, who can't figure out what's going on and secretly complains.

Fresh Living Dead: A Pair of "Great Rasus". Mr. and Mrs. Niu Lan were able to revive from a feigned death thanks to the fact that famous Chinese scholars and high-ranking officials of the Party and the State advocated humanitarianism. Indeed, China treats foreigners with respect for human rights everywhere. You come, and I retreat. You are tough, and I soften. You go straight to the point, and I am evasive and procrastinating. But foreigners don't respect human rights when it comes to us. What can you do?

If this year is still destined to try the suffering of floods once again, I think it's better to let the victims live or die on their own. Otherwise, the foreign wheat and flour bought with tens of millions of foreign debt will end up in the bellies of bureau chiefs and section chiefs. It's truly an offense to the gods and a violation of heavenly laws. It's unnecessary.

Shanghai has changed, reaching Luoyang. But now Luoyang is much calmer. Mount Lu and Guling have risen to meet the selection of outstanding people and auspicious lands. Some say that China will one day be forced to hold a meeting on the Pamir Plateau. I think this saying has great philosophical meaning. The Pamir Plateau is said to be the birthplace of the descendants of the Yellow Emperor. Trees that are thousands of feet tall have leaves that fall back to their roots. There's nothing strange about it. As long as this fall doesn't break your neck, then go back to the old nest to enjoy the cool breeze. What's the harm?

Cries of the Distressed

— Ge Chonglou

The domestically produced film "Humanity," which recently premiered, appealed on behalf of the general public who are starving, freezing, and helpless. Many people who watched it shed tears, just like me. It shows that everyone has a compassionate heart. In fact, the portrayal of the disaster area in "Humanity" is just a small fragment. The misery of the drought in Shaanxi (my hometown) cannot be fully described in a single article or film. The most tragic scene in "Humanity" is when, in order to save her dying grandfather, a woman sacrifices her own son in exchange for a little grain. This doesn't even mention cannibalism, friends eating friends, and relatives eating relatives, the so-called "exchanging children for food." During the most severe period of the Shaanxi disaster, it was not a rare occurrence.

But was the Shaanxi disaster, with its hundreds of miles of barren land and millions of deaths, entirely due to the weather? I want to boldly say here that, although the Shaanxi drought was due to lack of rain, most of it should be attributed to the local authorities' oppressive policies. Because they usually exploit the people so much that they have no savings, when there is even a slight drought, it becomes unmanageable. As far as I know, during the Shaanxi disaster, the farmers were selling their farm tools, while the Shaanxi authorities were buying large quantities of weapons.

The suffering of the Shaanxi people is unspeakable, and I feel unable to express it all. Finally, I want to tell the public that the drought in Shaanxi is getting worse. In Wugong County alone, the population used to be over 200,000, but now only 70,000 remain. And those good people have no choice but to sit and wait for death. I hope that the government authorities and compatriots across the country will unite to save the survivors.

Brief news: Today (30th), the Ping She Opera Troupe has been invited by the Qin Family Mansion to perform at the Great Eastern Theater. The repertoire includes "The Wagtail Temple", "Yutang Chun", "Drunkenness", "Empty City Stratagem", "New Changban Slope", etc., which will be quite splendid. (If it is he)

Nationally Made Factories Worth Introducing (14)

— He Gongxing

(Two) (Three) Marble Factories

Recently, Western-style wooden furniture often uses stone as the surface material, taking advantage of its whiteness and resistance to oil stains. Our country imitates Western wooden furniture, so we have to buy it. The annual loss is not small. Those with patterns are commonly called marble. Pure white ones are called Alum Stone. The ones from Italy are considered superior, followed by Japanese stone. In fact, marble is produced in Yunnan, China. The patterns are natural, and the nature is hard. It is not comparable to the so-called marble mentioned above. Moreover, the value is quite high. Now it is not easy to obtain large materials. It can only be used for inlays, screens, and hanging screens.

Our country has also produced stone materials used on Western wooden furniture in recent years. Alum Stone is especially abundant in Shandong. It is said that it was first discovered by Germans and then operated by the Japanese. When Qingdao was recovered, the mining rights of the mountain were also returned to the Chinese people. Patterned stone had to be bought from abroad. A few years ago, a Cantonese person named Tang went to Huzhou to mine stone and make stone powder. He unintentionally obtained a patterned stone mountain. Unfortunately, the color and pattern were not as bright and clear as foreign goods. Perhaps it was because it was mined from the surface. In the future, it may be better when excavated underground. The price is half that of foreign goods. The market price for rough pieces is five yuan per cubic foot. Polished stone, half an inch thick, costs two yuan per square foot. The Shanhai Marble Company on Edward Road in Shanghai is a mechanized manufacturer of this stone. Only this one in Shanghai is owned by Chinese people. Last year's business was worth over 300,000 yuan. The company also operates artificial stone business. However, many construction companies in Shanghai can make artificial stone recently. It has become a very common industry. No need to elaborate.

(Two) (Four) Cosmetic Factories

Our country has been famous for manufacturing cosmetics since ancient times. Reading the "Rhapsody on the Afang Palace," one can imagine the grandeur of Qin Palace's cosmetics. In modern material civilization, there are even more types of cosmetics manufactured. To list them all, there are almost three hundred kinds. There are countless cosmetic manufacturers in Shanghai. There are about eighty with trademarks and factories that can be investigated. However, the types of products they produce range from more than ten to seven or eight, and some only produce one or two. The amount of capital is not uniform because of the amount of products produced. The large ones have capital of over one million yuan, while the small ones only have dozens of yuan. Famous ones are Family, Guang Sheng, Yonghe, Xiangya and other factories. Famous products include Family Industrial Cooperative's Invincible Tooth Powder, Guang Sheng's Double Beauty Brand Flower Dew, China Chemical Industry's Samsung Brand Snow Powder, Yonghe Industrial Cooperative's Moonlight Goddess Brand Toothpaste, Sincere Company's Thousand Mile Fragrance, Meiya's Hair Beauty Lotion, Mainland's Elegant Box, China-France's Baby Face, China-West's Little Girl, and other Meixing Brand Fragrant Powder, Golden Bell Brand Hair Growth Oil, Banknote Brand Dusting Powder, Autumn Moon Brand Powder Puff, Student Brand Fragrant Honey, etc. There are many items. It is impossible to list them all. The total annual sales in this city are valued at 4 million yuan. The sales in other cities are 2 million yuan. According to the Customs Trade Register of 1910, foreign imports still amounted to more than 4.3 million yuan. The number is alarming. Now, if you manufacture cosmetics with small capital, you can still manufacture Snow Cream Vaseline, etc. Although tooth powder does not require much capital, you cannot make money without large-scale production and sales. The item of decoration is more important than Snow Cream. Only raw materials such as magnesium carbonate, talc, and peppermint extract can be purchased from domestically made goods. Since the release of domestically made tooth powder, the Japanese King Kong Lion Brand tooth powder has disappeared from the market. This can be said to be a success of resistance. It is gratifying.

Recording the Sounds of Old Temple Bells (59)

— Bu Chu Ting Cao Zhai Fu (Studio of Unweeded Courtyard)

Sixty-Six

The youths of the old temple have risen. Everyone has seen the one-year plan for children and seen the children actively following the plan. Not only do they feel a little itchy in their hearts, but even their hands are itching. As for myself, I am at the intersection of children and youth, but it is better to say that I am a youth than a child. I am holding a torch and burning everywhere. "Children have become a one-year plan, how can we youths lag behind?" Soon, the youths of the whole village held a meeting with great enthusiasm and passed the following one-year plan for the old temple youths: (1) Dig a well;

(2) Build a road to the city gate;

(3) Organize a youth afforestation association to establish a nursery, with each person planting at least 200 trees;

(4) Use new rice seeds to plant a field per person and try it out;

(5) Use new wheat seeds to plant a field per person and try it out;

(6) Learn a craft during the agricultural off-season, such as weaving cloth, weaving towels, weaving socks, etc., to increase production;

(7) Organize a youth martial arts club to learn twelve sets of boxing, and learn any one of knives, spears, swords, and sticks;

(8) Join the self-defense corps to complete the company training, practice field battles four times, and hit moving targets, with three consecutive shots hitting the target;

(9) Join the fly extermination team, mosquito extermination team, bed bug extermination team, and locust extermination team to cooperate with all the village children to eliminate pests in the entire village and nearby areas;

(10) Organize a cooperative;

(11) Organize a youth drama troupe to perform four times;

(12) Organize a youth concert, with each person learning one kind of musical instrument and five sets of songs;

(13) Recognize and use one thousand characters;

(14) Play fifty sets of scientific tricks and be able to explain the principles contained in each trick;

(15) Understand the movement of celestial bodies, day and night, the way of cold and heat, and the process of growth of one kind of plant and one kind of animal through observation in the field;

(16) Organize a youth newspaper and book club, with each person reading the newspaper every day and reading new books every month, and those who cannot read should learn quickly;

(17) Each person earns five yuan with their own labor for the purpose of recovering the three northeastern provinces;

(18) Voluntarily or nominate two or more people to join the volunteer army to recover the three northeastern provinces, with all the youths in the village jointly responsible for family support to avoid worries for the patriotic soldiers.

Supplement to the Shanghai Shen Bao

On Speech

Zheng Xiaoxu Speaks on the Politics of Ruin

— Fo

What Zheng Xiaoxu speaks of is originally a Japanized version of Kingly Way Politics, not the Politics of Ruin. In reality, how could Zheng Xiaoxu understand Kingly Way? How could he be worthy of speaking of Kingly Way? What he is worthy of speaking of is only the Politics of Ruin, as he is an experienced person who has personally been through it, so I call him as speaking on the Politics of Ruin.

The other day, a certain Qing loyalist returned from a visit to Puyi and described in detail how Puyi was being monitored by the Japanese in Changchun. He said that people call the Manchukuo a puppet government, but after my visit, I secretly fear that Xuantong is not even as good as a puppet, but is like Zhang Bangchang and the Emperors Huizong and Qinzong of the Song Dynasty. And Zheng Xiaoxu, like a gourd hanging without being eaten, is still giving lectures on his Kingly Way politics at the so-called Advanced Officials Training Center. It's truly a wonder that he can speak it out. That is why I say that Zheng Xiaoxu is only fit to speak of the Politics of Ruin, and not fit to speak of Kingly Way politics.

Puyi is called the Regent, but he is no different from a prisoner. Originally, he was not called Emperor but Regent, which was very meaningful. The "Zhi" in Regent originally meant "to seize," meaning to seize him and make him govern. Therefore, Puyi's every move and word is monitored by the Japanese. He has completely lost his freedom, like a student in a private school under the strict supervision of a stern teacher. Even when whispering privately with a classmate, he must look at the teacher's face. It is exactly the same. If he is not careful, the cane will follow. Puyi's current situation is like this. I wonder if he has realized it now? Is it more impressive than it was in Tianjin?

Zheng Xiaoxu urged the old master to simmer sand pots and encouraged Puyi to restore the monarchy, wanting to enjoy the addiction of being a prime minister. Now you can think back and wonder what it tastes like. Originally, his mind was filled with old Chinese history from when the Han borrowed from the Xiongnu, the Tang borrowed from the Turks, and the Song borrowed from the Khitans. Now he wants to use it to deal with the current environment. It's truly foolish, truly a dream. Now that you have tasted the taste, please continue to speak on the Kingly Way politics, or please speak on the Politics of Ruin.

Therefore, I was reminded of what a friend told me the other day. He also came back from outside the Pass. One day, a certain Qing loyalist went to visit Puyi and said, "The Regent must consult on his own, and great power cannot be allowed to fall into the hands of others." These words were heard by Komai, who immediately had him summoned for questioning. The Qing loyalist explained his words, saying that the so-called great power that cannot be allowed to fall into the hands of others refers to the entire Manchuria and that it should not be intimidated by the power of the League of Nations and changed. He was then forgiven and allowed to leave. Another Qing loyalist went to visit Puyi, fell to the ground, wept, and said nothing. This was also heard by Komai, who had him summoned for questioning. The Qing loyalist said, "I am so grateful that I am moved to tears and have nothing to say. Without the help of your country, where would Xuantong be today?" Komai smiled slightly and told him to leave quickly.

When I saw this news, I sighed three times in anguish!

Literature and Art

Visiting the Bund Park

— Song Fu

The ten-mile stretch of prosperity is foreign soil, a stroll in the park to enjoy the cool. Rolling waves churn up turbid tides, shady summer trees reflect weeping willows. Chinese and Western delicacies are arranged in abundance, clean white tablecloths are well-arranged. A continuous stream of tourists adds to the elegant atmosphere, with the coming and going of fan shadows and the rustling of clothing. Electric lights twinkle and add to the grand mood, the flowing music evokes passionate feelings. Here on the Bund, one can frequently gaze afar, one may as well indulge in wine and wander about drunkenly.

Farmers Yearning for Rain

Since summer began, it has been perpetually clear, farmers are tormented by the heat and feel distressed. No one in the suburbs is comforted by the hope of clouds and rainbows, in the three dog days they still ask for the blessing of rain. Let abundant sweet rain reward long-cherished wishes, generously bestow moisturizing dew and protect all living things. Building altars and setting up fasting services, the spirit of the gods protects, abstaining from killing and practicing vegetarianism, and following customary practices. Dragons appear in the rice paddies, a sign of good fortune, doves call on the willow banks, stirring joyous sounds. If Heaven truly follows the will of the people, the five grains will flourish and bring peace and prosperity.

Science

Methods of Making Black Pigments

— Ming

Black pigments such as lamp black, graphite, carbon black, drop black, etc., all contain a very high amount of carbon. They can be used to make agricultural and printing inks, paints, etc., and their uses are very wide. Their manufacturing methods are:

(1) Lamp Black: Place substances rich in carbon, such as oil, resin, coal black oil, ten-carbon dense cyclic matter, and sixteen-carbon dense cyclic matter, in a place with limited air and burn it to obtain lamp black. In fact, lamp black is soot, which on average contains 98 percent carbon. The quality is determined by the size of the powder.

(2) Graphite: Graphite is one of the carbon isomers. There are natural products produced in Sri Lanka, Siberia, Canada, the United States, etc. There are also man-made products. The method is to heat smokeless coal, bone charcoal or other amorphous carbon at high temperatures in an electric furnace with very little pressure to make artificial graphite. This is Acheson's Method. Both natural and artificial graphite contain impurities such as quartz, iron oxide, and alumina, but natural graphite contains more impurities and less carbon. Natural graphite contains about 60% carbon, while artificial graphite contains about 90% carbon.

(3) Carbon Black (i.e., Coal Gas Black) This pigment contains about 98 to 99 percent carbon. The method is to burn carbonaceous gases, such as natural gas or acetylene gas (C2H3), in a place with poor air circulation to obtain carbon black.

(4) Drop Black: This pigment includes Vine Black, Ivory Black, and Frankfort Black. Various raw materials, such as waste from ivory cutting, grape buds, cork cutoffs, coconut shells, etc., are heated in crucibles. The remaining residue in the crucible contains part of the raw materials, carbon, and minerals in the ash after burning. Most of the minerals are potassium salts, which can absorb moisture, so Drop Black must be rinsed and then dried. This pigment is extremely black. Compared with lamp black, lamp black becomes gray.

Office of the Releasing-Life Bureau

Society Improvement Discussion Association

Contributions to the Improvement of Men's Clothing

After reading Mr. Zhang Cangsu's proposal to improve men's clothing, I am deeply moved. I am eager to contribute some of my views.

Among the four major elements of life, clothing is very important. Although our country's clothing has undergone thousands of changes, with endless innovations, the basic long robe and short jacket remain unchanged. Apart from the fashionable Western suits and leather shoes, the old habits continue. All the problems have been stated by Mr. Zhang, so there is no need to repeat them. Now we have an urgent need to improve, but just talking without concrete measures, and without a detailed plan and discussion by the majority of people on what improved clothing is considered satisfactory and practical, it will not succeed. Now I am writing down my personal views: (1) Suitable Clothing: Clothing should be suitable for the body. If the length is not suitable or the size is uneven, it will affect a person's spirit and the cleanliness of their appearance. (2) Elegant Appearance: The appearance of clothing can show the awakening and decline of the national spirit.

(3) Economy: Our country is being invaded by strong neighbors from abroad and exploited by traitors from within, resulting in the exhaustion of the people and wealth. Therefore, we must strive to save money in terms of clothing.

(4) Simplicity: Clothing must be simple and convenient, and should not be too complicated and clumsy, so as to avoid stagnation in travel and waste of time in dressing.

Based on the above principles, I think the long robe should be shortened and the short jacket lengthened. The style should imitate the student uniform, but the collar should refer to the Zhongshan suit style. The trouser legs should be narrow and lengthened. Because Western suits are too complicated and wasteful, student uniforms are relatively simple, but the arms are not flexible enough. Central clothing feels loose and clumsy, so we should take the strengths of others and make up for our own weaknesses. The short jacket is lengthened and the collar of the central clothing is easy to collapse, so it imitates the Zhongshan suit style. The hips of Western-style pants are easily broken, so it is not as economical as the Chinese style of swapping two sides. I hope that my humble work is appropriate, and I ask the experts for guidance. This is respectfully submitted to the Society Improvement Discussion Association. Sincerely by member Xu Nangong,

Photograph of the school

New Student Enrollment

— Manqian

This is the general situation for school new student enrollment:

When new students come to take the entrance exam, they are generally wearing a proper straw hat and a long summer cloth gown. In their hands, one is holding a folding fan, and the other is carrying a package of examination stationery wrapped in newspaper. This genteel appearance is completely different compared to their true colors after being admitted to the school!

The quota for enrollment is two hundred students, but in reality, only one hundred and four people have registered for the exam.

Each applicant pays two silver dollars as a registration fee; in such hot weather, it's embarrassing for the school principal to ask the teachers and staff to supervise the exam and grade the papers as a mandatory duty. The principal has no choice but to grit his teeth, reach into his pocket, sweeten the teachers' mouths, and treat them to watermelon soda and a few tables of food and wine. This is to prevent them from complaining in private!

The physical education instructor is always paying attention: are there any athletes applying? If you've stood out on the sports field, it doesn't matter if your exam results are not good; in the end, you will still be on the list!

The school principal is paying attention: in the appearance of new students, if someone is dressed in a suit and leather shoes, with a modern attire, then the principal fears that you might be active and cause disturbances. No matter how well you do on the exam, there is no hope of being admitted! On the other hand, if you are rustic and full of country air, then the principals will express their twelve points of welcome and sympathy!

The first test is mathematics. By the time of the second test, physics, thirteen people were gone. By the time of the final oral examination, only eighty-two people remained!

Those who submitted blank math papers accounted for one-third of the total. Another third, although they scribbled something randomly, the result was still the same as not doing anything. The remaining third was relatively good, but none of the scores exceeded sixty points! As a result of the new student exam, only one person passed the overall average score, barely reaching sixty points. Only four people scored above fifty points. Because of this, it was difficult to set the admission standard. After several discussions, it was finally decided that all those with an overall average of thirty points or above would be admitted. However, calculating this way, there were only thirty-seven people. In the end, three more were added with an overall average of twenty-eight points or above, making a total of forty people!

Because the number of pre-determined enrollment slots was not filled, they had no choice but to hold the second and third recruitment rounds as much as possible. Of course, the situation was the same as the first recruitment.

Family Matters

Severing the Head

— Shiben

Xu Laoer, nicknamed Little God of Wealth, who lived next door, died of plague last night. During his life, he was diligent and thrifty, accumulating assets worth one hundred thousand. Because he was a money-loving entrepreneur, he never enjoyed good food or clothing in his forty-plus years. He only knew how to buy fields and houses year after year, increasing his assets. He never spared a dime for local public welfare or charitable causes. People saw his lack of benevolence despite his wealth, so although they nicknamed him Little God of Wealth, they secretly called him a miser.

Although he accumulated a lot of wealth, he still worried about having no heir when he died. Because he was not yet fifty years old, he still hoped to marry a concubine and have children. Therefore, he immediately refused the clan's suggestion to establish an heir to inherit his estate. But heaven has unpredictable winds and clouds, and man has good and bad fortune. Before he could achieve his goal of marrying a concubine and having children, he lost his vast wealth and died.

His sudden death without having arranged matters after his natural lifespan caused a great dispute. After the news of his death spread, the clan's nephews and grandsons ran over in droves, rummaging through boxes and cabinets, seizing property deeds. Everyone was fighting and grabbing, desperately trying to collect property. They were all like living robbers. They ignored his corpse, which had been lying on the bed for a day. Only after all the cash savings had been completely plundered by these nephews and grandsons did they remember that real estate was the right of the heir. Then, everyone gathered around to take care of his funeral for the sake of the property.

According to local customs, holding the head when the body is placed in the coffin is the duty of the heir, and it is considered a necessary indication of who will inherit the estate. Therefore, for those who have biological sons, there is naturally no issue with holding the head after death. However, if there is no heir, then the issue of holding the head often becomes chaotic and tumultuous. Now, Xu Laoer is in this situation. Several nephews, you want to establish an heir, I want to inherit, causing endless disputes. The quarrels continued until Xu Laoer had been lying on the bed for three days and had not been resolved. However, the summer weather is hot, and how can a corpse be left for several days? So, by the third day, when his nephews' head-holding issue had not yet been resolved, his corpse had already fulfilled the saying "a dead man in June rots quickly."

By the afternoon of the fourth day, this major issue still had not been resolved. However, the general relatives and friends all complained to the nephews, "You can argue over the inheritance after the coffin is sealed. You shouldn't make things difficult for the deceased." The nephews listened and thought that prolonging the matter was not a good thing, especially since the weather was hot, and the stench was overwhelming. If they didn't proceed with the burial, wouldn't the body turn into bloody water? So, they agreed to the relatives' request and ordered the gravedigger to change Xu Laoer's hat. However, after all the procedures were completed, when the gravedigger was carrying the corpse from the bed to the coffin, the nephews were all afraid of not holding the head, and thus not being able to seize the inheritance. So, they all rushed forward like a swarm, grabbing Xu Laoer's skull. In the chaos of many hands grabbing, the already decomposed skull, grabbed by more than a dozen hands, with a "thump" sound, Xu Laoer's means of making a living was severed from his body under the violence of his nephews' grabbing and pulling.

Alas! Poor Xu Laoer, after decades of hard work, he created an estate of over one hundred thousand, but in the end, he only ended up with his head severed from his body.
